Memorial from the Northern Fujian Fellow Townsmen Association 16

The delegation of petitioners from the Northern Fujian Fellow Townsmen Association in Beijing submitted a memorial to the Fourth Plenary Session, stating that Northern Fujian is located upstream and is close to Jiangxi Province. The communist bandits of Hunan and Jiangxi are now being pressed by the large army and will inevitably try to flee into Fujian. There are no heavy troops stationed there, and the remnants of the Lu bandits are scattered in various counties of Jianning and Shaowu. If the communist bandits and Lu bandits join forces, the suppression will never be completed. It is requested that a large army be dispatched quickly to enter Fujian from the sea or the Zhejiang border and be stationed in the Jianning and Shaowu area. Advancing, they can connect with the Jiangxi army to implement an encirclement; defending, they can also consolidate the defense of Fujian and avoid turmoil.

Zhang Xueliang Receives Chinese and Foreign Journalists 17

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang, Deputy Commander of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, received Chinese and foreign journalists in Nanjing at the headquarters at 11:00 AM on the 16th. More than 40 people attended. The reception was hosted by Zhu Guangshu, the Director of the General Affairs Department, and others. The journalists were asked to prepare several questions in advance for Zhang to answer. Zhang appeared in military uniform at 11:30 AM and greeted the journalists with a wave of his hand. Then, he answered the questions asked by the journalists one by one as follows:

(1) How to deal with the negotiations with Russia? Zhang replied that he would proceed in accordance with the spirit of the Sino-Russian and Fengtian-Russian agreements and by peaceful means.

(2) What about the national defense of Northeast China? He replied that this matter involves diplomacy and cannot be disclosed.

(3) How to deal with the aftermath of the Northern military affairs and how to deal with Yan Xishan, Feng Yuxiang and Wang Jingwei? He replied that the National Government has established permanent peaceful methods for the aftermath of the Northern military affairs. Regarding the handling of Yan Xishan, Feng Yuxiang and Wang Jingwei, Chairman Jiang and Xueliang have discussed it many times. Everyone should already understand the content. Xueliang absolutely obeys orders. If there is anything that cannot be done, he will ask the central government for instructions. Now that Yan Xishan, Feng Yuxiang and Wang Jingwei have left the country and gone abroad, there is absolutely no problem.

(4) What are your opinions on the generation of representatives to the National Assembly? He replied that the principle of convening the National Assembly has been approved by the Fourth Plenary Session, and the methods are being studied in detail.

(5) What are the measures for the reorganization of party affairs in Northeast China? He replied that they are exchanging opinions.

Zhang said at the end that he was sorry that he was unable to have a detailed discussion with everyone due to his hasty trip to Nanjing. He would be very willing to introduce to everyone the political, military, diplomatic, financial, educational, and construction issues of Northeast China in detail. However, due to time constraints, he could not report on it today. He would set a date to have a long talk with everyone after the Fourth Plenary Session closes. After Zhang finished his report, the meeting adjourned. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

Zhang Xueliang Visited the Mausoleum Yesterday 19

Chiang Kai-shek Gave Instructions to the Officers and Soldiers of Zhang Xueliang's Guards

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang visited Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum at noon on the 16th. When he arrived at the Mausoleum Park, he first took photos with Zhu Guangmu, Hu Ruoyu, and He Fenglin, and toured the surrounding mountain scenery. Chiang Kai-shek also arrived at 12:30 PM. He first took a short rest with Zhang in the ear room on the right side of the spirit hall, and then began the ceremony. At that time, the entire guard team, led by Commander Xu, advanced from the mausoleum road to outside the gate of the spirit hall. Zhang stood in the center, and the entourage was divided into two columns, one for civil and one for military. Chiang Kai-shek also stood on the left side to accompany the ceremony. Zhang personally presented a wreath. After the ceremony, Zhang asked Chiang Kai-shek to leave the auditorium and give instructions to the officers and soldiers of the guard team, expounding on the main points of the Three Principles of the People: (1) Anyone who does not uphold nationalism and does not have nationalistic ideas is not worthy of being a complete citizen. We soldiers must especially understand nationalism and be role models for being human. We must liberate ourselves from the oppression of imperialism and build an equal and free country. (2) Soldiers are protectors of civil rights, not oppressors of the people. If civil rights cannot develop, the country cannot be independent. When in the army, you can be good soldiers; when discharged, you can be good citizens, and be responsible for building the country together with the people and organizing society. If civil rights develop, it will not be difficult to build a sound country. (3) Soldiers build the country in order to seek a good life for the people. You also have parents, wives, children, friends, and relatives at home. Therefore, your hard work must be subject to extremely strict constraints, which is also for the good life of your own families. In short, the Three Principles of the People are for building the country, building people, and building soldiers. I hope that all officers will earnestly advise the soldiers and strive to practice the Three Principles of the People, so that they can be liberated from the oppression of imperialism. This responsibility rests entirely on our soldiers. I hope you will work hard. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

International Telecommunications Negotiations 24

Zhuang Zhihuan's Wireless Report

(Nanjing) Zhuang Zhihuan reported at the Central Broadcasting Station on the 16th on the negotiations regarding the revocation of the agreement on the unification of submarine cables of the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Pacific companies. The outline is as follows: (1) Prohibit submarine cable landings; (2) Cancel submarine cable patents; (3) Prohibit free sending and receiving of telegrams; (4) China has the freedom to stipulate submarine cable fees and transit fees; (5) Pay off the principal and interest of debts to facilitate negotiations. Regarding the Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations: (1) Open a submarine cable between Shanghai and Nagasaki; (2) Open a submarine cable between Qingdao and Sasebo; (3) Open a submarine cable between Chuanshi Mountain and Danshui; (4) Open a submarine cable between Yantai and Dalian; (5) Negotiate on telecommunications between Southern Manchuria and Japan. The above ten items will be discussed one by one. Currently, at the beginning of the negotiations, both parties are exchanging opinions on the Shanghai-Nagasaki submarine cable. The Japanese side also insists on its acquired interests and refuses to return them. Our side is arguing on the basis of reason and refuses to give up, so no concrete methods have been discussed yet. In short, the handling of international telecommunications negotiations this time is based on the principle of equality and mutual benefit, so that in the future, China's international telecommunications traffic can be free from all restrictions of unequal treaties, and can stand on a balanced footing with all countries in the world for development. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

Military Situation in Suiyuan 25

Zhang Chengde's Troops Will Be Stationed in Suiyuan

(Beiping) Guo Fengshan telegraphed a few days ago, representing Suiyuan, obeying the central government, and claiming to be the commander. It was later found that Guo and others were commissioned by Wang Zemin, the Shanxi military commissioner in Tianjin, as the Suiyuan Security Commander. The authorities telegraphed Zhang Xueliang to ask for instructions. Zhang replied that Guo Fengshan, Jin Guoying, Zhu Jiliang, Wang Guangxiong, Zhang Xiaoliang, and Zhu Ren sent a telegram from Tianjin, claiming that they were appointed by Wang Zemin and Jiang Yishan, the Shanxi military commissioners, as the Suiyuan Security Commander, cavalry and infantry division commanders. Wang and Jiang also sent a telegram from Tianjin Sanyuan Yi, claiming that the appointments were made after various procedures. Wu Tiecheng and Zhang Qun were entrusted to inquire about the origins, and they said that they did not know about this matter and could be ignored. It was found that the above-mentioned people were using false names and spreading rumors by telegram. The authorities should order their subordinates to investigate and prevent them strictly. If they take any actions outside the law, they should be immediately suppressed to avoid trouble. (Special dispatch on the 16th)

(Beiping) It is rumored that the central government will hand over the Suiyuan issue to the Northeast Army. It is planned to station Zhang Chengde's newly trained cavalry in Suiyuan. Debt Consolidation Committee Puts Forward an Outline of a Consolidation Plan 28

(Nanjing) The Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee submitted an outline of a consolidation plan to the representatives. The content is divided into eleven articles, which is a method of repaying debts to various countries annually starting from this year. However, the proposal did not specify the amount of repayment. It is also heard that our country's committee members also explained China's plan to allocate 5 million yuan from customs revenue to repay internal and external debts this year. Now that the military situation is largely settled, there will be a surplus in finances, and the amount allocated from customs revenue can be increased year by year, without being limited to 5 million. Foreign Important Telegrams

Japanese Prime Minister Hamaguchi's Condition Still Not Out of Danger 65

Acting Prime Minister Shidehara Narrowly Escapes, Jiangmu and Andatsu Factions Secretly Feud

▲ United Press of Japan, Tokyo, 16th The condition of Prime Minister Hamaguchi deteriorated temporarily last night. Yesterday evening, the nurse on duty suddenly came out of the sickroom and reported the Prime Minister's condition to the attending physician, Mr. Manabe, in a low voice. Mr. Manabe looked very shocked and immediately entered the sickroom to examine the Prime Minister in detail with Dr. Shioda. Then, except for the two doctors and Mrs. Hamaguchi, her two children, all were asked to leave the sickroom. The ministers who came to express their sympathy to the Prime Minister also waited for the announcement in the next room. At 9:00 PM, the two secretaries, Mr. Nakajima and Mr. Toda, carefully consulted and then announced the Prime Minister's condition at 10:00 PM. It can be seen that there was a major change in the condition at that time. The atmosphere inside and outside the sickroom was quite tense for a while. Dr. Shioda told reporters at 11:00 PM last night: "When I examined the Prime Minister at 6:00 PM this evening, there were slight signs of problems in his chest. The more this kind of phenomenon occurs, the more dangerous it becomes. If the body temperature is the highest and the breathing and pulse are not disordered, then it can be regarded as optimistic. At present, the gas in his abdomen has not yet been released. He was injected with a sleeping drug once at 9:30 PM.

▲ United Press of Japan, Tokyo, 16th Dr. Shioda announced Prime Minister Hamaguchi's condition as follows: "The stomach was washed at 8:00 AM on the 16th, and gastric juice containing bile was washed out, which seemed to be quite comfortable. If this condition continues for two or three days and no gas is produced, there should be no concern." At 9:00 AM, the pulse was 95, the body temperature was 37.6 degrees, and the breathing was 15. At noon, the body temperature was 37.5 degrees, the pulse was 97, and the breathing was 18.

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 16th The appointment of Foreign Minister Shidehara as Acting Prime Minister is of course the result of Minister of the Army Ugaki's illness, but behind the scenes there are still complex relationships within the Cabinet and with the party. This is because the heroes do not give way to each other, so the neutral Shidehara was elected. It can also be said that Shidehara gained this position by chance. Within the Minseito Party, the secret struggle between the Andatsu faction and the Jiangmu faction is quite fierce. Andatsu has a great influence in the general election. Jiangmu, the Minister of Railways, is the mastermind of Prime Minister Hamaguchi and also has an invincible force. No matter who of the two serves as the Acting Prime Minister, it will shake the party. On the night when Prime Minister Hamaguchi was assassinated, the two factions were quite active in secret. Seeing this situation, Minister of Railways Jiangmu immediately used lightning-fast means to tell Prime Minister Hamaguchi and invited Minister of the Army Ugaki to understand, and first obtained Shidehara's approval, and then personally proposed to the Cabinet to elect Shidehara, and without waiting for Shidehara's approval or disapproval, he pushed him to be the Acting Prime Minister. The inside story is like this, so Shidehara's acting is only temporary. If Prime Minister Hamaguchi needs some time to recover from his illness, he will be subject to political considerations again, especially since the opening of the Diet is imminent, which makes Shidehara even more uneasy. As for what strange strategies the Jiangmu faction will come up with, it is impossible to guess. The Andatsu faction's nerves are tense for it.

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 16th Although Prime Minister Hamaguchi's condition is progressing very smoothly, it will still take a considerable amount of time for him to fully recover. However, there is only one and a half months left before the Diet convenes. If Prime Minister Hamaguchi cannot attend the Diet in person, the opposition parties' attacks will be concentrated on Shidehara's concurrent position as Prime Minister, and communication with the ruling party and other matters will be hindered. Therefore, there is a lot of dissatisfaction within the Minseito Party with Shidehara's acting Prime Minister. Some people advocate introducing a Cabinet member from the party to replace the vacant post of Prime Minister in order to reorganize the lineup. If this proposal becomes a concrete development, it will cause disputes in the party's power relations. It is worth paying attention to the extent to which this atmosphere will develop.

Crisis Lurks in the Spanish Situation 66

All Industries in the Capital Declare a General Strike to Protest the Security Team's Shooting and Injuring Workers

Traffic Stops... Shops Close

▲ Reuters, Madrid, 14th Today, the funerals of the four people who were crushed to death when a seven-story building collapsed were held, and 50,000 people carried the coffin. The authorities prohibited them from passing through a certain street in the busiest part of the city, resulting in a conflict with the police. The police, unable to resist the crowd, opened fire in self-defense, killing four people and injuring many more, including 11 police officers. As for the cause of the collapse, it is said to have been caused by the negligence of the engineer and the contractor. The construction industry has declared a general strike until Sunday.

▲ Guomin News Agency, Madrid, 15th Since yesterday's conflict between construction workers and the security team in the Spanish capital, a bloody incident has occurred, resulting in the death of five workers and the injury of more than 40 workers and police officers. Today, a general strike has been declared. The labor union insists that the captain of the security team, who did not give a warning before suddenly ordering to fire, be dismissed and that more than 100 arrested workers be released. The authorities seem determined to use force to suppress the strike, so the situation is extremely serious. Residents are extremely frightened and are hoarding food in preparation for emergencies. Many shops are also closed. Striking workers are marching in teams in poor areas, shouting slogans such as "Down with the King" and "Overthrow the Government." There are also reports of strikes and riots in Barcelona, Valencia, Cordoba, and other smaller cities outside the capital. Furthermore, the railway workers across the country are demanding a pay increase and are threatening to strike. Another telegram states that the strike leaders in the Spanish capital have just announced that the workers in public utilities and bakeries will go on a general strike for 24 hours, and the workers in other industries will go on strike for 48 hours. In the afternoon, students joined the workers' march, causing many conflicts to occur in various places. In the evening, the entire city was plunged into darkness, all traffic was suspended, and the army was preparing in the barracks. The labor union committee has notified the workers to strictly maintain order. Newspapers have suspended publication, so rumors are spreading like wildfire, and people's hearts are even more volatile.

Balkan Alliance 69

Will Have Important Developments

▲ Reuters, London, 15th A message from Constantinople says that the ambassador to Turkey left for Rome yesterday to participate in the talks between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and the diplomatic authorities of Italy and Turkey. This shows that the important development of the Balkans is further advanced. It is said that this development was promoted by Greek Prime Minister Venizelos. After touring various European capitals in 1928, Mr. Venizelos went to Ankara, the capital of Turkey, to sign the Treaty of Friendship and the naval limitation agreement between Greece and Turkey. At that time, commentators believed that an important step in the negotiation process had been reached. Not long after, Hungarian Prime Minister Bethlen visited Ankara, and rumors abounded, saying that Turkey, Greece, and Hungary would launch a Balkan alliance under the guidance of Italy to resist French imperialism in Eastern Europe. However, Mr. Venizelos denied this, saying that his goal was to form a free and friendly alliance of the Balkan and Near Eastern countries. British Economic Policy Unchanged 70

MacDonald's Speech at the Labor Party Congress

▲ Reuters, London, 16th British Prime Minister MacDonald said at a Labor Party rally in Bedford last night that no British government can absolutely assure overseas autonomous territories that the British people can tolerate economic policies that will reduce foreign trade or impose taxes on food and raw materials used by factories. He does not adhere to free trade or other doctrines, but in today's fierce competition, some situations will inevitably depress the standard of living. This is a fact. This situation does not come from free trade countries, but from protectionist countries with gradually lower wages. No matter how advocates of import tariffs argue, no one with knowledge can say that tariffs can maintain a high standard of living and enable the people of protectionist countries to maintain a standard of living that meets humanitarian standards. He believes that a government that encounters such difficulties should have a sense of security. He does not believe that a general election is necessary at present, nor does he believe that the people of the country currently want a general election.

Domestic Important News

The Depression of the Sino-Russian Conference 74

▲ Mo Dehui is in a Dilemma in Russia ▲ The Future of the Conference Awaits Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang's Decision

▲ Four Newly Appointed Special Commissioners Postpone Their Trip to Russia

Harbin Dispatch: Since Wu Zesheng returned home with his mission to report on the Sino-Russian Conference, there has been no news here. The Directorate General of the Chinese Eastern Railway occasionally receives a telegram from Moscow, but the sentences are incomplete and mostly unimportant, so the Directorate General suspects that the Russian side is checking the telegrams and intercepting them. Previously, Mo was already prepared to return home, but he was instructed by a telegram from the Central Government to postpone his departure from Russia so that the Russian side would be responsible for the breakdown of the conference, and he was allowed to allocate 30,000 yuan for the delegation's expenses. As a result, Mo suspended his return to China. A few days ago, he telegraphed the diplomatic messenger Fu Zhanwen to send him leather clothes quickly and to purchase enough food for three months. However, the special commissioners Tu Weiseng and Li Chen left Russia a month ago and are still living in Paris. If there is no definite date for the resumption of the conference, these people will not return to Russia. Karakhan and Mo Dehui met informally once last week. They did not discuss the conference in depth because Russia would not allow concessions on the Boli Conference records, and we did not express any recognition. The meeting was just a friendly meeting. A certain important person in the Railway Council here received a letter from a secretary in the delegation the day before yesterday, which contained words related to the Sino-Russian Conference, roughly saying, "At present, the responsibility of Plenipotentiary Mo is quite difficult. If he returns home hastily, it will be a minor matter to delay diplomatic relations, and a major matter to reopen the border conflict. It is useless to stay here without returning home. Whether the conference can open up a new situation depends on the attitude of our Central Government and whether or not it recognizes the Boli Agreement. Since the Central Government has no detailed instructions to Mo, Mo is in a dilemma. Mo himself is extremely anxious, and we, the attendants, also feel that the future is bleak." This shows Mo's difficult situation. Yesterday morning, Wu Zesheng returned to Harbin from Liaoning. I went to inquire about the attitude of the highest authorities in the Northeast. He said that Commander Zhang Xueliang must go to Beijing to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek before a decision can be made. The Central Government is still largely ignorant of the conference situation. After the meeting, a suitable solution can be discussed. If so, the future of the Sino-Russian Conference does not lie with Russia or Mo, but depends on the meeting between Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang. Because there is no definite date for the resumption of the conference, Wu Zesheng and the four newly appointed special commissioners Qian Tai, Zhang Shou Zeng, and others have postponed their departure. The diplomatic messenger Fu Zhanwen will go to Russia on the ninth of this month to deliver winter clothes and food first. All the opinions about the Northeast were sealed in several letters and handed over to Fu by the Commissioner of the Border Defense Department to take away. Yesterday morning, Jin Ronggui, a counselor at the Directorate General of the Chinese Eastern Railway, went to Shuangchengbao and returned to Harbin in the evening. It is vaguely heard that Jin's mission is to visit Cai Yunsheng on behalf of Mo Dehui and ask Cai to mediate with Russia and help from the middle so that the conference situation will not remain so depressed for a long time. Cai and Mo have a relationship as in-laws, so they may be able to help. In diplomatic practice, there is no personal friendship involved, but Cai and Russia seem to be a different matter. (November 11th)

The Russian Influence on the Chinese Eastern Railway is Gradually Expanding 75

▲ Preliminary Plan to Exclude Chinese Employees Through Examinations ▲ Reducing Chinese Laborers and Replacing Them with Russian Laborers

Harbin Dispatch: The Soviet Union's operation of the Chinese Eastern Railway has used a chain-style plan in recent years. After one plan is implemented, another plan emerges, one after another. Since Mo Dehui is not in the country, the authorities are struggling to cope. After the deadlock in the Translation Department of the Railway Bureau, the Russian Director of the Railway Bureau proposed to the Council to implement examinations for all road engineering, mechanical, and rolling stock professionals throughout the road starting in January next year. All staff currently serving in the various engineering, rolling stock, and mechanical offices must take the exam, and only those who pass will be allowed to work in the Railway Bureau. If this method is implemented, at least thousands of Chinese employees will lose their jobs due to the exam. Chinese employees with specialized knowledge are originally few, and they are able to serve in various places because they are proficient in Russian language and speech and because they are rich in experience. The Russian side wants to achieve its ambition to control road affairs, so it excludes Chinese employees by means of examinations. Acting Chairman Li Geng, in the interest of the Chinese side, negotiated with the Russian friends and advocated waiting for Mo Dehui to return home to convene a formal meeting of the Council to decide. It is expected that this matter will not only violate the Feng-Russian Agreement but also affect the interests of the Chinese side and will inevitably become a dispute. In addition, the Russian Director also plans to reduce the room expenses and pensions of road employees in January next year, saying that it is to save expenses. The current salary system of the Chinese Eastern Railway is that each employee, in addition to receiving a monthly salary, is allocated a number of official rooms according to the amount of his salary. Those who do not have official rooms to live in are given 25% or 30% of their monthly salary for room expenses. Those who have been working in the road for many years and apply for retirement are given pensions, the amount of which is proportional to their length of service and salary. The road funds used for these two expenses each year are quite a lot. If they are reduced, it may not be a way to save money. However, it is heard that the Russian Director's intention is to reduce them uniformly on the surface, regardless of Chinese or Russian, but in reality, he will increase the salaries of Russian employees and pay them the original amount, and only reduce the amount paid to Chinese employees. This matter is related to the interests of more than 8,000 Chinese employees, and it is predicted that it will also become a major problem. Before the Railway Bureau plans to implement these two things, it has already started to cut Chinese laborers. The method is quite cunning. At the moment, there is a batch of Chinese laborers who are voluntarily resigning without leaving any traces of Russian repression. That is, 200 Chinese laborers in the Thirty-Six Zha were transferred to the Dieling Iron Factory to serve. The original salary of each worker was 2 yuan per day. After being transferred to the new factory, they would receive less than 8 jiao per day, and once they were transferred, the original amount of pension would be canceled. Most of the Chinese laborers have served for more than 20 or 30 years, and the amount of their pensions is not small. Naturally, they are unwilling to transfer to the new factory job and abandon their huge pensions, so they all resigned. After the Russian Director resigned the Chinese laborers, he transferred 200 Russian laborers from Hailar to fill the number. It is heard that the second and third batches of transferred Chinese laborers are being prepared. It seems that we have no words to protest this kind of passive conspiracy to reduce Chinese laborers. It is heard that since July, no less than 2,000 Red Russian employees have been added along the line. Their intentions are far-reaching. They want to gradually reduce the Chinese influence. (November 10th)

Lu Diping Stationed in Zhangshu to Supervise the Suppression of Bandits and Communists 76

▲ Zhu Mao's Rout to Nancheng and Shicheng

Nanchang Correspondence: Lu Diping, Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Government and concurrently Commander-in-Chief of the Ninth Route Army, has, with the successive recapture of Shanggao, Qingjiang, Xingan, Xinyu, Fenyi, and other counties by the First, Second, and Third Columns, and with Zhu Mao's forces, except for a portion entrenched in Ji'an, fleeing eastward in Jiangxi, urgently needing to be annihilated as soon as possible, led the headquarters of the Ninth Route Army and the First and Fifth Aviation Teams to Zhangshu this morning to direct operations. Accompanying him were Chief of Staff Xie Muhan, Secretary Cao Zhicai, Adjutant Tan Yinzhi, and dozens of others, as well as hundreds of members of the Provincial Government Guard and the Public Security Bureau Security Team. Lu took a Caisse aircraft to Zhangshu, and the other three aircraft also flew to Zhangshu at the same time, awaiting Lu's orders. Lu's staff and guards departed by motor vehicle on the Nanchang-Zhangshu road. It is heard that after Lu's arrival in Zhangshu, in addition to directing various units to attack Ji'an and recover the counties along the Gan River, he also plans to inspect the counties in western Jiangxi that have been afflicted by bandits. The duties of the Ninth Route Army Commander-in-Chief will be temporarily assumed by Chief of Staff Xiao, and the duties of the Provincial Government Chairman will be temporarily assumed by Committee Member and Secretary-General Yang Mianzhong.

Regarding the current situation of bandit suppression, after the main force of Zhu Mao moved to Chongren and Yihuang, attempting to flee to the Fujian border, the government troops also moved eastward to follow and pursue. The Gong and Luo Divisions are currently in Shanggao and Xinyu, and the Tan, Zhang, and Xu Divisions have a portion in Qingjiang and Xingan, and a portion advanced from Chongren to Fuzhou, joining forces with Deng Ying's Division. The battle lines stretch from Shanggao and Fenyi in the west, crossing the Yuan River and the Gan River in Xinyu, Qingjiang, Xiajiang, and Yongfeng, to Chongren and Yihuang in Fuzhou, a distance of several hundred miles. According to news from various sources in recent days, the main force of Peng and Huang is currently in Ji'an, Xiajiang, and Anfu, and the main force of Zhu Mao is in Chongren and Yihuang. The vanguard troops fleeing to Fujian have already reached Shicheng. Fuzhou was previously very dangerous, but after Tan's Division, Luo's Brigade, Zhang's Division, and Wang's Brigade arrived in Fuzhou from Zhangshu on the 14th, the situation has turned from danger to safety, and the bandits dare not attack Fuzhou. Currently, the troops of Deng Ying, Wang Jiejun, and Luo Shouyi are advancing towards Chongren and Yihuang to suppress them. Battles have broken out in Tangpu and Qiuxia. Firelight can be seen from Huangjiangkou, presumably due to the bandits burning houses. It is also reported that another part of the Communist bandits has reached the vicinity of Nancheng. Judging by their intentions, they will again flee from Ruijin to Tinghang. Lu has telegraphed the Fujian authorities, requesting them to quickly send troops to block them in western Fujian, to prevent them from escaping. (15th)

The General Situation of the Remaining Troops of the Jin Army 77

▲ Factional Disputes: Xu Yongchang Unable to Command

Beijing Correspondence: I traveled to Shanxi on business and stayed in Taiyuan for two days before returning to Beijing on the 12th. Along the way, I saw that the Jin Army on the Zhengtai Railway had Huolu as its front line, but only three companies were stationed there. Jingxing also had only a little over one battalion. Niangziguan had about two divisions, belonging to the Feng Pengzhu and Li Fuying units. Yangquan had about one division stationed, Shouyang had three regiments stationed, and Yuci had one regiment stationed. Inside and outside Taiyuan City, including the troops of Garrison Commander Rong Honglu and the remnants of various units that had retreated, there were at most only two or three thousand men. However, there were many military divisions, brigades, and regiments. Even those called divisions numbered more than ten. After the Jin Army's total collapse on the Henan and Shandong battlefields, in addition to those killed, wounded, and captured during the fighting, four or five out of ten deserted along the way. The number gathered in Shanxi province was generally small. However, those killed, wounded, and deserted were soldiers, not officers. Nine out of ten regimental commanders and above were unharmed. Therefore, after returning to Taiyuan, they still retained their original designations. Yan sent out twenty inspectors last month to go to various armies to inspect them. As a result, those who claimed to be an army had only several thousand men, those who claimed to be a division had only about a thousand men, and some who claimed to be a regiment had only one or two hundred men. Among them, the units that retreated from Shandong, such as Qin Shaoguan, Feng Yuxi, and Zhou Shilian, suffered the heaviest losses. After the inspectors reported back to Yan, Yan sighed and declared to the generals that their designations would remain unchanged, but military pay would be issued based on the actual number of personnel, and not based on the original designation. According to someone who spoke to me, the actual number of Shanxi troops currently existing is approximately as follows: 1. Sun Chu's unit, over five thousand men; 2. Yang Xiaou's unit, three thousand men; 3. Guan Fuan's unit, over four thousand men; 4. Wang Jingguo's unit, nine thousand men; 5. Li Fuying's unit, six thousand men; 6. Li Shengda's unit, two thousand men; 7. Feng Pengzhu's unit, four thousand men; 8. Yang Chengyuan's unit, four thousand men; 9. Yang Yaofang's unit, one thousand men; 10. Zhao Chengzhou's cavalry, five to six thousand men; 11. Zhou Dai's artillery, one thousand men; 12. Du Chunyi's guard brigade, five thousand men; 13. Other scattered remnants, totaling about three or four thousand men. Yan's remaining strength is only this much. However, Yan still wants to preserve these embers, so he pretended to retire and appointed Xu Yongchang as the commander of Jin-Sui, in order to maintain the remnant situation. However, Xu deeply knows the factional disputes within the Jin Army and has repeatedly declined, not daring to take office. When Zhang Xueliang arrived in Tianjin, Xu originally planned to go to Tianjin to meet with Zhang to discuss the aftermath, but just before his departure, many leaflets and slogans such as "Support Zhao Daiwen," "Support Fu Zuoyi," and "Down with Xu Yongchang" suddenly appeared in Taiyuan City. Xu then stopped. When Yan heard about this in Wutai, he immediately sent Gu Renfa and Shang Zhen to comfort Xu and invited Zhang Peimei to mediate, urging the generals to consider the interests of the Jin clique and cooperate with Xu. However, among the Jin figures with potential influence today, one is Zhao Daiwen, one is Wen Shouquan, and one is Shang Zhen. Zhao has his own plans and pleads illness when things happen. Wen is still in Shenyang. Shang has always been passive. If these three do not sincerely help Xu, I am afraid Zhang Peimei's mediation may not have any effect. (November 12th)

▲ Discussing the Reorganization of Railway Administration Issues

Xuzhou Correspondence: The Ministry of Railways believes that the vehicles of the Jinpu, Jiaoji, Longping, and Pinghan Railways were used the most during the military period and should be reorganized to improve railway administration. A few months ago, personnel were sent to conduct inspections and investigations. Now, Kang Deli, Chen Tao, Xu Changyin, Huang Lin, Tu Tang Dehua, and others have been dispatched to Xuzhou to convene a meeting of the four routes to discuss the reorganization of vehicles. Huang and Tang arrived in Xuzhou on the 8th, and Kang, Chen, and Xu also arrived in Xuzhou tonight (14th). The personnel sent by each route are: for the Jinpu Railway, Chief of the Car Management Department She Xu, Chief of the Audit Section Zhao Zonglian, Chief of the Car Section Zhang Youwei, Chief of the Locomotive Section Cheng Huating, etc.; for the Jiaoji Railway, Head of the Transportation Section of the Car Management Department Cao Changlin, staff member Cao Yi, Chief of the Locomotive Section Yang Heng, Chief of the Car Section Su Bubin, etc.; for the Longhai Railway, Chief of the Car Management Department Huang Fenggang, Deputy Section Chief of Xuzhou Xiao Xinwu, etc.; for the Pinghan Railway, Deputy Section Chief of the Car Management Department Jin Kewu, etc. They have also arrived in Xuzhou and are currently in contact with each other. It is expected that the meeting will be held on the 16th, after the Transportation Command completes its closure on the 15th. The Transportation Command has also drafted nine measures for reorganizing the vehicles of each route and submitted them to the headquarters for approval, to be proposed and discussed at the meeting. (14th)

Anhui Provincial Government Revised Grain and Rice Tax Rates 79

▲ All Military and Other Additional Taxes Abolished ▲ Tax Payments Now Calculated Using the Decimal Yuan System

Wuhu Correspondence: Rice and grain are the main products of Anhui, with annual exports of no less than ten million shi. Therefore, rice tax also accounts for an important part of the Anhui provincial treasury revenue. The export rice tax rate in this province has been traditionally set at 1 fen 4 li per shi for the regular tax. After Anhui entered the military period during the National Revolutionary Army's Northern Expedition, the authorities added a temporary military fee of 5 fen per shi to the export rice tax. Although the military period has ended, this temporary additional rice tax has not been explicitly abolished. The Guangchao, Yanning, and other rice merchants stationed in Anhui, as well as the Wuhu General Chamber of Commerce, have repeatedly appealed, but have not been granted. In addition, there is an additional 1 fen 1 li 4 hao for the road debt fund, so each shi of rice exported currently requires a tax payment of 7 fen 5 li 4 hao. For other miscellaneous grains such as vegetables and wheat, the regular tax is 7 fen 5 li per shi, which, together with the road debt fund, totals 8 fen 2 li 5 hao. Although Anhui has had a bumper harvest this year, many other provinces have also had good harvests. As a result, the Guangchao, Yanning, and other merchants have not yet boldly purchased, and the rice market is sluggish, which is unprecedented. However, the prosperity and decline of various industries in Anhui have always depended on the rice market. If the rice market is weak, all industries cannot function. The newly appointed members of the provincial government, in order to take care of merchants' difficulties and revitalize the market, have recently decided at the provincial government meeting to abolish all additional taxes on rice, grain, and other miscellaneous grains. For ease of calculation, the tax will now be calculated using the decimal yuan system, based on the provincial land tax silver to yuan conversion rate, with each tael of silver converted to 1.5 yuan. The export rice tax rate is revised to 2 jiao 4 fen per shi, and the miscellaneous grain tax is 1 jiao per shi. Regardless of whether it is shipped by sail or steam, the new rates will take effect from November 11th of the 19th year of the Republic. In addition to the public announcement, the Wuhu General Chamber of Commerce has also been notified to inform all rice merchants. (14th)

Wuhu Quick Report 80

▲ Qiupu County in southern Anhui was captured by Shao Shiping's bandit gang from Jiangxi on the 5th. They searched every household, causing losses of approximately one hundred and tens of thousands of yuan throughout the city. More than twenty residents were killed. The provincial government dispatched troops to suppress them a few days ago, and they were eventually driven back, and the county seat was recovered.

▲ The Ministry of Finance has reassigned Yuan Jiapu, Director of the Anhui Finance Department, to concurrently serve as Anhui Finance Special Commissioner. Yuan came to Wuhu from Anqing the day before yesterday, took office on the 13th, and returned to the province today. Luo Jieqiu and Luo Peiwei have been appointed as chiefs of the second and third sections, respectively. Everything is currently being finalized, and it is planned to move the special commission to the province within a few days.

▲ The rent resistance movement in Wanchun Township, Wuhu, has not yet been resolved. Yesterday, the county government sent the arrested Cui Qifa and others to the province for review. It is heard that the provincial government strongly advocates strict handling of this case and has appointed Qi to come to Wuhu to handle it. The county government and the Sixth District Bandit Suppression Command have issued announcements, ordering that rent be paid at a rate of 140 catties per mu. If there is further resistance, troops will be sent to the countryside to forcibly collect rent.

▲ The Wuhu-Datong small steamship, which was robbed previously, suffered losses of over ten thousand yuan. The Sixth District Bandit Suppression Command cracked a bandit den in Ju Zhi'an the night before last, capturing several bandits and a pistol. This morning, a company of troops was sent on a special Wuhu-Datong steamship to Digang, capturing six male and female bandits and recovering many stolen goods. (14th)

▲ Former Finance Special Commissioner Bao Geng went to Shanghai on business a few days ago and only returned to Wuhu yesterday. Unexpectedly, at 3 a.m. this morning, the Municipal Public Security Bureau suddenly received an order from the provincial government stating that Bao's accounts were unclear and ordering him to be detained immediately. The bureau sent personnel to Bao Geng's residence and invited Bao to the bureau, where he is temporarily residing pending orders.

▲ It is heard that Provincial Government Chairman Chen Diaoyuan will go to Beijing in the next few days due to important official business. (15th)

Local Correspondence

Nanhui 81

A Pirate Robbery Occurred in Nicheng Township: Nicheng Township, under the jurisdiction of the county, was suddenly attacked by more than thirty pirates armed with shucking guns at midnight yesterday. They went to the Sun Jinzhang and Hu Tianzhang stores, broke down the doors, and robbed them. Approximately three thousand yuan in cash was stolen. The police squad stationed in Henggang Township, about five li from the town, rushed to intercept them upon hearing the alarm. The two sides exchanged fire for more than two hundred shots. The pirates, unable to withstand the attack, retreated and fled southward by boat towards the sea.

Two Zao Hong Business Owners Kidnapped: Shen Guanjin, a business owner north of Zao Hong Township, was forcibly kidnapped by seven or eight bandits last night. Shen struggled and tried to escape by swimming, but was recaptured by the bandits. They took him south along the East Sea beach. The bandits left a note demanding a ransom of one hundred thousand yuan. The military and police are currently searching for them, hoping to solve the case.

Wuxi 82

The Finance Department Sends a Telegram Urging Limited Payment of Treasury Funds: Wuxi's assigned quota for the 19th-year customs short-term treasury bonds is 140,000 yuan. The county government's finance bureau has already reported and paid 110,000 yuan in several installments, with a remaining balance of 20,000 yuan that has not been paid. Yesterday, the Finance Department sent a telegram to Zhuang Yeguang, director of the finance bureau, ordering him to pay the full amount within three days to facilitate remittance.

Forced Divorce, Wife Killed with a Knife: Zhang Borong, a 24-year-old resident of Zhangjingqiao Township (Huai Shang Shi) in the seventh district, married Yan Aizhen, a 26-year-old, and they were very devoted after the marriage, having already had two sons. Recently, Zhang Borong suddenly became infatuated with a woman named Xiuqin from Bashiqiao, so he abandoned his old love for a new one. The day before yesterday afternoon, Zhang Borong sent someone to Yan's family in Zhaimen, falsely claiming that his wife was ill. Yan's father, Yan Xingchun, believed it to be true and rushed to Zhang's house to visit. Zhang Borong immediately forced a divorce. When Xingchun refused, Zhang rushed to the kitchen, grabbed a kitchen knife, and without asking why, suddenly slashed at his wife Yan Aizhen's head. Family members rushed forward to dissuade him, but she had already been injured in the neck, and blood was flowing profusely. Later, both sides went to the Seventh District Office for judgment. Since District Chief Zhao was busy in the city, the matter was not resolved.

Changzhou 83

Three Kidnappers Apprehended: According to a tip-off, the fifth branch of the Wuyi Zhengluqiao Public Security Bureau reported that the notorious bandit Cai Hubao (nicknamed "Little Tiger") specialized in kidnapping and extortion. Many farmers have suffered from his actions. Cai Rongsan, who sat and divided the loot, and Cai Aoda, who delivered threatening letters, were also his accomplices and were currently hiding in Caijiatang, about three li east of Zhengluqiao Township. Upon receiving the report, the branch chief, Jiao Jianping, immediately led a team of officers and police to Caijiatang to arrest them. Cai Hubao, Cai Rongsan, and Cai Aoda were all captured without resistance. After interrogation by the branch chief, Jiao confessed to having committed one kidnapping. The other bandits cunningly denied it. Yesterday (15th), a document and confession were prepared, and the arrested bandits Cai Hubao and others were sent to the county for trial.

Jiangyin 84

Pigs of Changfa Merchants from Hangzhou Robbed: The Changfa pig business in Hangzhou recently sent partners to northern Jiangsu to purchase hundreds of pigs on five or six boats. The day before yesterday, when passing through Qixugang in Jingjie, they were suddenly attacked by pirate boats. Eighty-eight pigs were robbed, leaving only thirty. Clothes, bedding, and rice were also looted. On the 14th, the boat entered Huangtiangang in Jiangyin to pay taxes. They also telegraphed tax stations along the Grand Canal and in Wuxi and Changzhou, requesting that any pig boats of that description be detained.

Changshu 85

17,500 Yuan in Cash Robbed En Route: The manager of the Yukang flower business in Hejiashi sent his partner Chen Mingkui to the city the day before yesterday (14th) to withdraw cash from the Bank of China. The bank conveniently handed over 17,500 yuan in banknotes. Chen Mingkui carried the money back to the village that evening on a Zhizhang ferry boat. However, Zhizhang is still several li away from Heshi. After arriving at the dock, one must disembark and walk. Unexpectedly, when Chen was walking near the Zhudian Bridge, he was suddenly surrounded by many robbers. They threatened him in every way. As a result, all the cash was robbed. Chen ran back to the store and reported the robbery to the manager. They then reported it to the fifth branch of the Public Security Bureau in the jurisdiction, requesting an investigation. The bureau has now dispatched a detective team led by Zhu Shunxiang to the countryside to investigate.

Bureau Chief's Gambling Raid Unsuccessful: Every year when the autumn harvest season arrives in this county, a group of idlers open gambling dens to absorb farmers' income, charging a heavy commission. The stakes are also high. Gamblers must be introduced by someone, and the dens are constantly changing locations to prevent information from being leaked. The most sophisticated gambling den is called "Lao Zuo." Recently, there have been rumors in society that certain institutions are providing subsidies. When Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Kunshan heard about this, he was very angry. The day before yesterday, he went out alone to the third garrison and led several patrolmen to Cao's house in Nanqingtang near the South Gate to raid a gambling den. (Cao's house is "Lao Zuo"). But the information was leaked long ago, and the internal structure of Cao's house was very winding. They were unable to find anything and returned in disappointment.

Nantong 86

Joint Water and Land Defense Conference Held: The joint defense of Nantong, Haimen, Chongming, and Qidong counties is scheduled to be held in Tongcheng on the 20th. Section Chief Zhang of the Fourth District of the Wusong Water Police, Team Leader Gong of the Seventeenth Team, Team Leader Lin of the Eighteenth Team, and the magistrates of Rugao and Changshu counties are invited to attend the conference.

County Magistrates Go to the Provincial Capital for Questioning: Yan Diannan, the former chief of the county police team, was captured by the provincial authorities and handed over to the military law division of the security department for trial. He denied any wrongdoing or harming the people. Director Li specially summoned the county's eighteen district chiefs, who were the original complainants, to the provincial capital for questioning. On the 15th, the district chiefs gathered in the city and decided to go to Zhenjiang as a group to await questioning, bringing all the relevant documents to request restrictions on the allocation of provincial funds. The annual busy canal and deed tax in Tongyi totals 154,578 yuan. The provincial government has consistently allocated more than 200,000 yuan annually. The shortfall has been covered by local funds, which is a significant amount. Currently, various groups have jointly petitioned the provincial government, requesting restrictions on the allocation of funds in order to provide relief.

Zhenjiang 87

Transfer of Public Security Bureau Chiefs of Huaiyin and Other Counties: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs yesterday dismissed Zhao Zhenhua, chief of the Huaiyin County Public Security Bureau, and transferred Zhu Ying, chief of the Songjiang Public Security Bureau, to succeed him. To fill the vacancy in Songjiang County, Shen Jing, chief of the Baoshan County Public Security Bureau, was transferred. The Baoshan County Public Security Bureau was reorganized into a section.

Finance Department Reassigns Business Tax Directors of Seven Counties: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance has reassigned the business tax collection registration fee directors of seven counties, including Lishui. It was learned yesterday that Lin Tonglun has been appointed as director of Lishui County, Zhou Fangquan as director of Dongtai County, Hu Yuanpei as director of Xinghua County, Xu Qijin as director of Haimen County, Chen Mingcheng as director of Jingjiang County. Wan Bingduan, the director of Dongtai County, has been transferred to Wujin County, and Quan Mingbao, the director of Jingjiang County, has been transferred to Nanhui County.

Jiaxing 88

The Department Sends Someone to He to Investigate the Case: Dai Weizong, an inspector from the Department of Civil Affairs, arrived in He from the province the day before yesterday. The next day, he investigated various administrative matters with various agencies and public organizations. It is also known that Inspector Dai's major mission to He was because a certain agency in Hecheng was accused of wrongdoing. Therefore, the provincial government specially appointed Committee Member Dai to come to He to investigate each item in detail to serve as a basis for review. Therefore, Dai's whereabouts indicate that he will need to stay in He for several days. After each item has been investigated, he will immediately return to the province to report.

The Provincial Commission Comes to He to Urge Tax Payment: Jiaxing's past years' grain tax has been severely undercollected. Although the county government has urged officials to go to the countryside to collect taxes, the effect has been minimal. The reasons are (1) He has suffered consecutive years of famine, and the people have little savings. (2) Many businesses lease out land in exchange for grain rent. If the rent is not received, it is difficult to pay the grain tax. Due to these two reasons, grain tax collection has not improved. However, the provincial treasury urgently needs funds and has repeatedly telegraphed the county government to expedite tax collection. Zhu Zhaoping was also assigned to He yesterday to oversee the collection.

Zhu's Regiment Also in Charge of Suppressing Bandits in Shengzhou: The bandits in Shengzhou, eastern Zhejiang, are rampant, causing disturbances in the areas bordering Xinchang and Zhuji. Wu Zhulong, commander of the Sixth Regiment, personally led the suppression, and on the surface, they seem to have been dispersed, but they have not actually been wiped out. Ningbo 90

Bandit Leader Executed by Firing Squad: Yuan Danyun, a bandit from Xinchang, was 31 years old this year. In September of this year, he became a bandit in his hometown. On October 19th, he gathered more than 300 people and confronted government troops at Tangtouling. He was captured by Wu Conglong's unit of the Sixth Security Regiment, sent to the Ningbo Bandit Suppression Command, interrogated thoroughly, sentenced to death, and the sentence was submitted to the provincial government for approval. Yesterday afternoon at 1 p.m., Yuan was brought to the execution ground on Ben Cao Road in Jiangbei and executed by firing squad.

Robbery at a Wedding: At the home of Zhang Afa in Zhang Village near Guisi Bridge in the Zhenhai West Administrative District, the wedding was celebrated the day before yesterday. It was quite lively, with many guests congratulating them. At about 1 a.m., seven bandits suddenly arrived, armed with clubs and knives. Three of them were on guard, and four entered the house and looted for an hour. Approximately more than 300 yuan in cash, a leather box containing more than 70 yuan in banknotes, more than 10,000 copper coins, a pair of pearl rings, two gold rings, a gold lock piece, and clothes were stolen, totaling a loss of 700-800 yuan.

Xiaoshan 91

Ministry of Education Bans Religious Propaganda in Schools 95

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, strictly prohibiting missionary schools from propagating religious doctrines. The original notice stated: "With reference to a letter from the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee, regarding a petition from the Nanjing Municipal Executive Committee requesting the National Government to instruct the Ministry of Education to strictly prohibit religious subjects and religious ceremonies in all missionary schools to prevent cultural aggression, etc., the instruction was: 'Investigate and reply, return the original documents to the Ministry of Education.' In addition to investigating and replying to the previous case, the original petition is copied and sent to you for investigation and handling." It also attached the original petition. "Private schools, if established by religious organizations, must not make religious subjects compulsory and must not engage in religious propaganda in class. If there are religious ceremonies in the school, students must not be forced or persuaded to participate. Religious ceremonies must not be held in primary schools. These regulations have been clearly stipulated in the regulations for private schools and have been repeatedly ordered and strictly enforced by the Ministry." "Local educational administrative agencies should have already strictly inspected and separately dealt with the schools established by religious organizations under their jurisdiction." "Now, with reference to the previous instructions, in addition to replying and distributing the notice, you are hereby ordered to submit a detailed report on the handling of the matter. At the same time, you should continue to supervise your subordinates and pay close attention to the propagation of religious doctrines in schools established by religious organizations. If there are any violations, they should be strictly prohibited and reported at any time. Do not neglect this order."

Ministry of Education Orders Schools to Report New Students and Faculty 96

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued a notice to the education departments of various provinces (except Shandong), national universities, colleges, specialized schools (except the Shanghai National Conservatory of Music), and municipal education bureaus (Shanghai and Nanjing): "Regarding the registration books of new students and transfer students admitted by various schools in the 19th year, along with graduation or study certificates and faculty rosters, which were previously ordered to be reported to the Ministry within one month according to Instruction No. 1026, the deadline has now passed." "It has been found that the schools in your province have not yet submitted them, which is a violation of the Ministry's order. Considering that the military situation has just stabilized and transportation may be inconvenient, the deadline is extended by another month. You are ordered to follow the previous order and promptly forward the report. Do not delay any further." This order.

Ministry of Education Urges Submission of University Student Survey Forms 97

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued a notice to the education departments of ten provinces, including Hebei, and the education bureaus of three cities, including Shanghai: "Regarding the status of students in national universities in the 18th year, the Ministry previously issued survey forms and ordered each department to distribute them to the provincial and registered private universities or independent colleges under their jurisdiction for completion and submission within the deadline." "Subsequently, it was noted that a small number of schools had failed to comply with the order, and a list of the non-reporting universities or independent colleges under their jurisdiction was copied and sent with an order to urge them to submit the forms. The relevant statistics are now urgently needed for compilation and evaluation." "It has been found that the student status of the aforementioned universities, etc., has not yet been reported to the Ministry. In addition to distributing the notice, you are hereby ordered to immediately investigate and comply with the previous order, complete the forms by the deadline, and submit them directly to the Ministry. This is of utmost importance." This order.

Zhejiang Education Department Promotes the National Phonetic Alphabet 98

The Education Department of the Hangzhou Municipal Government believes that education authorities everywhere are actively promoting the National Phonetic Alphabet, and that public education in particular should emphasize this teaching method. Therefore, it has specifically drafted a practice book format for the National Phonetic Alphabet and requested the Education Department to issue a notice to all public education institutions in various counties and cities to adopt this practice book. The Education Department believes that this practice book is excellent and suitable, and has ordered the education bureaus of various county and city governments to forward the notice for adoption, and has also instructed the municipal government to take note.

General Situation of Education in Baoying County 99

Mr. Jin Yingyuan, an investigator from the Joint Preparatory Office for Compulsory Education in Various Counties of Jiangsu, investigated the general situation of education in Baoying. The following is an excerpt:

The director of education in Baoying County has been changed seven times in the past three years, which inevitably affects the entire undertaking. There are many accumulated arrears over the years. The reasons are: first, the expansion of undertakings exceeded the budget; second, there were two years of famine, resulting in a shortage of tax revenue (with the collection of 51%, the shortfall is estimated at more than 90,000 yuan). The accumulated arrears before the 15th year of the Republic were 21,550 yuan, the accumulated arrears in the 16th year were 66,000 yuan, and the accumulated arrears in the 17th and 18th years totaled approximately 91,960 yuan, totaling 179,510 yuan. The future remedial measures are: in terms of increasing revenue, starting from the 19th year, a request has been submitted to increase the general education land tax by two cents per mu, which is expected to generate 22,000 yuan. An increase in the tax quota is expected to generate 3,000 yuan, totaling 25,000 yuan. In terms of reducing expenditure, starting from the second semester of the 18th year, the budgets of various schools, museums, and administrative offices have been reduced by approximately 16,800 yuan. The budget for the 19th year has been reduced by approximately 22,800 yuan. If the two cents per mu of general education land tax that was not levied in the 19th year is collected, along with the tax quota increase and the budget reduction, the total will be 47,800 yuan. If the shortfall in tax revenue is gradually collected, the accumulated arrears can be cleared within two or three years, and the situation will improve. Director Zhou Songnan has only been in office for two months and is very enthusiastic about raising funds. He successively established the budget for the 18th year in July and the budget for the 19th year in August. New undertakings include: in terms of compulsory education, in addition to adding eight primary schools, ten classes have been added. In terms of general education, the county junior high school has added one grade, and the county No. 2 primary school has added one grade. In terms of social education, two public education centers, one simple library, one public education experimental area, and twenty-four public schools have been added. A farmers' education center is currently being prepared.

(1) Finances: The budget for the 19th year has greatly reduced expenditure. Regarding revenue, the surtax and collection taxes are 81,285 yuan, the surtax is 3,300 yuan, the special tax is 4,446 yuan, the miscellaneous taxes are 4,700 yuan, the property tax is 26,700 yuan, the tuition and boarding fees are 4,100 yuan, and the temporary income is 3,200 yuan, totaling 127,731 yuan. Regarding expenditure, the educational administrative expenses are 9,787 yuan, the general education expenses are 22,911 yuan, the compulsory education expenses are 43,194 yuan, the social education expenses are 22,994 yuan, the special income is 2,000 yuan, the contingency fund is 6,105 yuan, and the second contingency fund is 17,685 yuan. The county's educational expenditure was more than 3,000 yuan per month before the 16th year of the Republic. After the 16th year, the monthly expenditure suddenly increased to 8,300 yuan. In the second semester of the 18th year, the monthly expenditure was reduced to 5,500 yuan. This year, due to the increase in undertakings, the monthly expenditure is 7,000 yuan.

(2) Compulsory Education: The county is divided into four school districts, with a population of 358,000. The number of school-age children enrolled is 2,270, and the number not enrolled is more than 58,000. There are 51 primary schools with 92 classes, costing 29,808 yuan. There are 620 private schools with 13,245 students. The number of students in each primary school is more than 30 for those with many students and 11 or 12 for those with fewer students, which seems to be a large difference from the number stipulated by the department. Each school also has a kindergarten class (with four rectangular tables and 12 or 16 people sitting around them). According to the investigation, most of them have reached school age and should be incorporated into the first grade for classes. As for children who have not reached school age, if there is no kindergarten to accommodate them, at a time when compulsory education funds are tight, there are as many as 50,000 school-age children in the county who are out of school, and it seems that rescuing these children who have not reached school age is still in the second step. The county's teachers include 39 graduates from normal colleges and senior high school normal departments, 22 graduates from old-style middle schools and senior high schools, 69 graduates from rural normal schools and county normal schools, 17 graduates from A and B type normal training classes, and 11 qualified testers. In the future, if funds are increased, one is to increase the land tax by two cents per mu, two is to measure school land and increase the rent, and three is to rectify miscellaneous taxes to increase the contract amount. For teacher training, it is planned to invite Yangzhou Rural Normal School to run a class every year. The survey of school-age children is still in the planning stage. The current compulsory education funds are used for consolidating old undertakings, amounting to 22,228 yuan, and for new undertakings, amounting to 9,998 yuan, with no savings. The general education land tax of 8 cents per mu has been finalized, and 6 cents has been collected. If the 2 cents that have not been collected can be realized, it seems that it should be fully retained and gradually promoted in rural education.

(3) General Education: There is one county junior high school in the city, with four grades (boys and girls are divided into groups in the third grade), 160 students, and 25 faculty members, with annual expenses of 9,600 yuan. The equipment for physics, chemistry, and natural sciences is very simple. The newly appointed principal has not yet taken office. There are three county primary schools with a total of 11 grades, one private Dunmu primary school with two grades, and one Lucun primary school jointly run with Yangzhou Middle School with one grade, totaling 14 grades. According to the investigation, there are many private schools in the city and countryside, and students often surpass primary school and enter high school midway. It is said that this trend has not diminished and may hinder the progress of compulsory education.

(4) Social Education: The county is divided into four public education zones, each with a public education center as the center. The first public education center is in the city, with 23 staff members and annual expenses of 6,876 yuan. The organization is divided into library, lecture, sports, promotion, science, art, general affairs, public reading room bi-weekly magazine editorial department, wall newspaper society, etc. There are a total of 24 active undertakings and 25 fixed undertakings. The second public education center is in Sheyang Town, divided into library and lecture departments, with monthly expenses of 82 yuan. The third public education center is in Sishui Town, divided into lecture, library, sports, and promotion departments, with an attached public library, with monthly expenses of 150 yuan. The first public library is in the city, divided into selection, cataloging, guidance, and administrative sections, with monthly expenses of 78 yuan. The number of daily visitors is very large. Other examples include the first zone of public schools with seven schools and eight grades (including women's classes), the second zone with two schools and two grades, the third zone with five schools and five grades, and the fourth zone with two schools and two grades, each school with monthly expenses of 15 yuan (once every four days). In addition, there is a joint improvement public teahouse in the north of the city. The county has all kinds of social education facilities. If it is not just an expansion of undertakings and seeks to enrich the content, it is truly good news for the future of social education. (The following is omitted)

Deng Weifu Returns Home After Completing His Studies 103

Deng Weifu, from Changsha, Hunan, studied in Belgium. In 1928, he graduated from the Civil Engineering Department of the National University of Ghent in Belgium. Master Dong Renjian's Speech 104

The World Chinese Students' Federation invited Master Dong Renjian to give a speech yesterday afternoon at 7:00 PM entitled "The Bankruptcy of Chinese University Education." Mr. Zhu Shaoping chaired the meeting. The main points of Mr. Dong's speech are as follows: (A) Reasons for the bankruptcy of university education: (1) The general society's boredom with university education; (2) University education does not improve with social needs; (3) Fierce competition; (4) Lack of talent; (B) Impact of the bankruptcy of university education: (1) Official bureaucratization; (2) Professor commercialization; (3) Student politicization; (4) Professor non-specialization. The results of this impact: (1) Unclear school-running goals; (2) Complex curriculum; (3) Disordered training; (C) Relief of the bankruptcy of university education: (1) Promote specialization; (2) Scholars govern the school; (3) Improve treatment; (4) Protect human rights. The speech lasted for an hour. After the speech, the audience stood up to thank him and dispersed.

Portugal Defeats Luanhua 107

The Result is a Ratio of Eight to Two

The Luanhua and Portugal teams were at the bottom of the Westerners Association Group A standings with zero points each. Yesterday, the two teams played at the China Baseball Field. It was expected beforehand that the two sides were evenly matched and there would be a fierce battle. However, in the battle, Luanhua was clearly inferior, losing two goals in five minutes. The score was six to two in the first half. In the second half, Portugal scored two goals. As a result, Portugal won by eight to two.

▲ The Portuguese Team Fights Fiercely with Ten Players 108

Ten minutes after the start of the first half, Portugal's right inside guard, Gang Shierfu, was injured and left the field. Afterwards, they fought with only ten players, but their momentum did not weaken. Luanhua not only failed to take advantage of the opportunity to win, but was scored four goals by Portugal. Luanhua only scored two goals. Before the end of the first half, Luanhua's Li Ning was injured in the face and also left the field to rest. From the beginning of the second half, each side fought with ten players, and the situation became more balanced. The lines became more disorganized and uninteresting. Before the end of the game, the audience left one after another.

▲ Luanhua Obtains a Free Kick 109

Luanhua started the attack first. Portugal intercepted the attack. Right wing Xun Na rushed forward. Li Ning was about to step forward to compete when Xun Na passed to the front of the goal. The Portuguese center forward obtained the ball. Yang Renwei blocked the ball. The ball bounced to the right side. Fafanqie kicked the ball and scored the first goal. Not three minutes later, Portuguese center back Gu Shitan made a long shot from the left wing position and surprisingly scored a goal. Portugal was now winning by two goals.

Afterwards, Luanhua counterattacked. Portuguese right inside guard Gang Shierfu was injured and left the field. The strength of the back line was slightly weaker. Luanhua obtained a free kick next to the penalty line in front of the Portuguese goal. Li Huitang kicked the ball in. As soon as this ball went in, Portugal launched a major attack and scored another goal. After competing for a long time, Luanhua suddenly became brave. Five forwards surrounded the Portuguese goal. The Portuguese goalkeeper ran out to save the ball. A melee ensued. The ball suddenly fell in front of the goal. Wang Jihuai lightly pushed the empty goal, and the ball slowly rolled into the goal, making the score three to two.

▲ The Portuguese Team Wins the First Half with Six to Two 110

After the center kick-off, Luanhua suffered another heavy blow. Gu Shitan passed to the left wing, and then passed to the front of the Luanhua goal. Fafanqie coordinated from the middle. The right wing stepped in and kicked the ball in. The two Luanhua defenders were on the side, not stepping forward to compete, which was also a strange thing. In the next five minutes, Fafanqie scored two goals in a row. Luanhua's Li Ning was injured and left the field at this time. The first half ended immediately. Portugal won by six to two.

▲ The Lineup is Not Perfect in the Second Half 111

From the beginning of the second half, the lineups of each side were not perfect. Portugal scored one goal each by the Kolaisha brothers in the first quarter of an hour. From then on, it was messy and perfunctory until the end. Portugal won by eight to two. The referee was Jiang Xiangqing. There were about 3,000 spectators. The lineups of the two teams are as follows:

▲ Portugal: Ge Tish, Maisaier, Gang Shierfu

CR: Fafanqie, Gu Shitan, Fafanqie; HAS: Alun Sen, Fafanqie, Kolaisha, Kolaizhou, Xun Na

▲ Luanhua Team: Lu Zhongen, Li Ning, Qian Yaobin

Emerging New Japanese Tennis Players 117

▲Singles Player Sato (Naotaka) Defeats Old Sato (Taira) of the Davis Cup Three Straight

▲Doubles Team Sato (Taira) and Abe Eliminated Early in the Davis Cup

(Tokyo Correspondence) Recently, Japan held the 9th National Tennis Championship competition. More than 40 veterans and rising stars in the national tennis world participated in the competition. Among the Davis Cup players, reason for singles play and Ota were unable to participate due to matters. Sato (Taira), who served as the Davis Cup doubles player, volunteered to join the singles competition and participated in doubles with his original partner Abe.

Among the singles players, the most promising are naturally the veteran Sato (Taira), the Far East representative Sato (Buhei), and the 口 (name missing) who once defeated Sato (Taira). After several eliminations, the two Satos were left to hold the final battle on the 10th. As a result, the young Sato (who defeated Lin Qiu in the Far East Games) conquered the newly returned Davis Cup player, old Sato, with scores of six to four, eight to six, and six to two in three straight sets. The old Sato's serve was quite skilled, the position of the ball landing was also very good, and he was able to win with a calm attitude. It is a pity that the performance was not fully demonstrated. The young Sato is powerful, runs smoothly, and is especially capable of chasing and saving dangerous balls. He often returns the dangerous ball unexpectedly, making the enemy at a loss. If he can pay more attention to calmness, his future is limitless.

In the doubles, in addition to the Sato (Taira) and Abe team and the Yamagishi and Shimura team who attended the Far East Games, the Sato (Naotaka) and Kawachi team are the most promising. Unexpectedly, in the semi-finals, the Sato and Abe team was defeated by the little-known Kobe Commercial University Buhei and Kuwabara team. The latter also had smooth sailing and competed with Yamagishi and Shimura for the championship. Yamagishi and Shimura have been partners for many years, and their contact skills are very proficient, so that the enemy has no gaps to take advantage of. Buhei was originally known for his singles, and his personal technique was excellent, but Kuwabara repeatedly gave the enemy opportunities to take advantage of, and became the target of the enemy's attack, eventually leading to defeat. The result was four to six, six to four, six to three, and six to four.
