Party and Government Agencies Strictly Order Silk Mills to Resume Work 120

Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association, Chairman Shen Huachen, Standing Committee Member Zhu Jing'an, etc., after going to the capital to request the government to issue silk industry public bonds, returned to Shanghai. Because the suspension of silk mills throughout Shanghai affected the livelihood of workers, a general meeting of all colleagues was specially convened to earnestly persuade manufacturers to find ways to resume work to maintain workers' lives. At that time, 32 companies were found who were willing to work hard to start work, but wages had to be reduced appropriately to reduce the burden. After the 11th, the factories separately convened meetings of employees to inform them of the situation of temporarily reducing wages and working hard to start work. The employees in each district understood the difficulties and were willing to cooperate sincerely. Therefore, the employees of the silk mills in each district went to work as usual without any objection. However, the nine silk mills, including Yuanfeng in the Hongkou District, announced the start of work the day before yesterday. Chen Zongxiang, an employee of Yichang, ordered all employees to sign a statement prohibiting machinists from starting fires, and threatened the factory owner. He was detained by the police and sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for detention. Personnel from the Party, government, and police agencies in the city were dispatched to find out the truth and ordered Chen Zongxiang to be detained for strict handling. At the same time, the nine silk mills were advised to resume work immediately, and the police were sent to protect them. It is now known that yesterday was Sunday, and each silk mill should have suspended work. The nine silk mills, including Yuanfeng, all prepared in accordance with the order and decided to resume work on the 19th. Yesterday, the industry association notified all employees to check. Yesterday afternoon, the East District Workers' Union held a special meeting at Changshi School to discuss ways to rescue Chen Zongxiang. The three Party, government, and police agencies in the city also jointly issued a notice yesterday and posted it in front of each factory to prevent further disturbances. The notice is copied below: Shanghai Special City Party Department Mass Training Association, Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Notice No. 4067, Joint Notice, According to the Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association's report, the nine silk mills, including the Hongkou Yuanfeng Silk Mill, were advised by the association to start work on the 15th of this month. Unexpectedly, the Workers' Union convened the machinists and stokers of the nine silk mills in Hongkou, who are now planning to start work, and threatened them not to start fires and not to issue motive power, claiming that the twenty silk mills in Hongkou must start work at the same time, and cannot only start nine. Chen Zongxiang led many people to the home of Wu Gensheng, the foreman of the Yuanfeng Silk Mill, to prohibit him from starting a fire and forced the employees in the factory to sign a statement prohibiting work. Fortunately, the third office of the fifth district of the Public Security Bureau detained Chen Zongxiang. It was found that the employees and female workers of each factory have all understood, but the Workers' Union has come out to obstruct work, please investigate and handle it. It was found that the silk industry in this city was forced to close down due to the sluggish silk market. Now that we are working hard to find ways to open the factory, the responsible persons of the trade union should understand the difficulties and work together. But they are using this as an excuse to threaten and deter the resumption of work, which is very unreasonable. The council is deeply concerned about the sluggish silk market, which affects the suspension of silk mills and the lives of workers. For the future of the silk industry, we will take both into consideration and strive to ensure that both labor and capital get their due. I hope that you workers will accept the advice, resume work on a specific day, and if there are valid reasons, you will be allowed to submit them for verification. The overall goal is to take care of the lives of the workers and ensure that they can work with peace of mind. Anyone who obstructs work will be immediately arrested and severely punished. It is urgent to inform everyone to obey and not to disobey. This is the notice. Chen Junyi, Standing Committee Member, Yuan Liang, Director, Pan Gongzhan, Director, November 15, 19th year of the Republic of China.

Petition of the National Private Electric Power Association 122

▲Government agencies must not hold provincial-run power plants again

The National Private Electric Power Association submitted a document to the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang to petition, saying, (omitting titles) "Respectfully reading Premier Sun Yat-sen's industrial plan, the focus of running industries is on food, clothing, housing, and transportation. Supplying household electric lights is designated as a type of residential industry. Furthermore, the outline of industrial and commercial administration states that preparing for large-scale private factories is to implement Premier Sun Yat-sen's military industry policy, but the state cannot hold private industrial and commercial enterprises that have already achieved success to avoid competing with the people for profit, etc." Electric power undertakings include electric lights, electric heating, and electric power. Electric lights and electric heating are supplied for household needs, and electric power is supplied for various motive powers, which is sufficient to improve life and increase production. Therefore, all private power plants should be maintained and promoted to promote their development. Last year, the private power plants across the country were taken over by the government one after another due to the Qi Shuyan Zhenhua Power Plant and the Hangzhou Dayouli Power Plant. Feeling a sense of imminent crisis, representatives were elected to come to Beijing to petition. The government listened to public opinion and promulgated the Regulations for the Supervision of Private Public Utilities and the Regulations on Electric Power Undertakings, the Registration Rules, etc. There are clear provisions regarding the business term and region to prevent disputes. Therefore, the maintenance of private electric power operators is complete and thorough. Unexpectedly, this year, the Guangdong Provincial Government overstepped its authority to reorganize the Guangzhou Commercial Electric Power Company, and the Zhejiang Electric Power Bureau has a plan to officially run a large power grid. The management rights, regional rights, and business rights of private companies are sufficient to cause great panic among private power plants, making them unable to operate with peace of mind. It has been repeatedly reported that official-run large power plants are actively proceeding with Gengzi indemnity and electrical public bonds. The location of their establishment is nothing more than in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang area. It is found that there are more than 100 private power plants in each province in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, which shows that the people of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are leading the way and are still working hard to invest in private electricity. As long as the government provides guarantees and urges them to proceed, it is not impossible for private power plants to form a power grid, and government agencies can transfer their financial resources to other provinces that have not yet been established. Isn't it convenient for both parties? Otherwise, private operation in the front and official operation in the back is very easy to cause disputes. This year, our association sent representatives to Germany to attend the World Power Conference and investigate the electric power situation in various countries. We learned that its nature is purely private and local management. The term of the year has no time limit, or the shortest is 40 years, and the legal protection is even more thorough. As for state-owned, only the Soviet Russian government. It is found that the military affairs have come to an end, and the central government is determined to repair the internal affairs and promote industry to cultivate the national capital. Private power plants have been losing money due to years of war and commercial depression. If they are not actively maintained, it is difficult to avoid bankruptcy. Therefore, the reasons are briefly stated, and I beg you to maintain and protect the laws and regulations that have been promulgated for private electric power. I urge you to increase the term of the year to improve and expand the business as much as possible. To the area where private power plants have already been established, the country should not hold them again in the same area or nearby locations to dispel doubts. Whenever there is a need for reform, government agencies can only provide guidance or supervision on the law and cannot overstep the bounds to manage them to protect property rights. It is enough to uphold the Premier's industrial plan and conform to the main purpose of industrial and commercial administration. Presumptuously stated, I beg your judgment. The National Private Electric Power Industry Federation bows and deletes."

Postal Workers Continue to Drive Away Liu and Oppose Savings 128

The Shanghai Postal Workers and Employees Associations, after the expulsion of Liu Shufan, Director of the Postal Service, and the opposition to the establishment of a special bureau for postal savings and remittance, pushed to its breaking point, sent representatives to Beijing to petition together with Comrade Wu Kaixian of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department. When the central government and the supervisory, administrative, and legislative branches expressed their sincerity and accepted the representatives of the two associations, they returned to Shanghai to report and listen quietly to the central government's handling. It is now reported that the two associations have been holding meetings for a long time and have not received any instructions from the central government or information on how to handle the matter. The two associations held a meeting for many days and resolved to submit a petition to the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang to seek to implement the two major goals of expelling Liu and opposing savings. When necessary, they must continue to send representatives to the conference to make a final struggle. It is said that the petition has been drafted and will be issued today. In addition to the points mentioned in the petitions to the Central Party Department, the National Government, and the various branches of the two associations as reported in the previous newspapers, it is also stated that Liu's claim that "citing the successful methods of various countries and requesting the establishment of a special bureau for savings and remittance" is actually fabricating facts and deceiving the central government. According to the investigation by the trade union, there is no special bureau for savings and remittance in various countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, France, and Germany. The one separated in Japan is only a part of the savings, and the department has repeatedly separated and merged with the post office for 30 years. Even now, although there is a situation where the savings and deposits are too large and the establishment of a special bureau is insufficient to manage them, some people still advocate that although the post office and savings may be separated in theory, they must be merged in fact. Therefore, Liu's request to separate the special bureau for savings and remittance is only for the purpose of expanding his personal power and arranging private affairs, and there is no consideration for the future of the post office and savings and remittance.

County Reorganization Committee Explains the Number of Representatives of the Chamber of Commerce 137

The Training Department of the Shanghai County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee notified the Party departments in each district yesterday, stating that the Training Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee issued Order No. 142, which opened with, "Now, the Training Department of the Nantong County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee has sent personnel to request an explanation of Article 1 of the Chamber of Commerce Law regarding the member representatives of the Chamber of Commerce. Each chamber shall send one representative, but if its average number of employees in the most recent year exceeds fifteen, it may add one representative for every fifteen additional employees. What exactly is meant by 'average number of employees in a year'?" Based on this, after investigating, the "average number of employees" mentioned in the original article should, in accordance with Article 8 of the Implementing Regulations of the Chamber of Commerce Law, the number of representatives of members of the Chamber of Commerce should be calculated by combining the total number of employees of the stores affiliated with the Chamber of Commerce. Of course, it refers to the average number of people employed by the stores affiliated with the Chamber of Commerce as a whole. For example, if the total number of people employed by ten stores affiliated with a certain Chamber of Commerce is over 150, then its average number of employees exceeds fifteen, and it can increase the number of representatives according to the regulations. If the total number of employees used by the ten stores is less than 150, then the average number of employees is below fifteen, and there is only one representative, etc. Because this matter involves explanation, it is urgently notified to all concerned.

Qujia Bridge Homicide in Luodian 147

▲ The Murderer Refuses the Sentence ▲ Filed an Appeal Yesterday

Zhou Wang, a farmer in Qujia Bridge, Luodian, Baoshan, was 29 years old. In the spring of this year, she became acquainted with Qian Jisheng, a local fisherman. Not long after, she was sold to Zhang Shengrong as his wife by a matchmaker. Unexpectedly, only seven days after arriving at the Zhang family, her former lover, Qian Jisheng, went to the Zhang family with a knife on the evening of the 16th of last month and stabbed Zhang to death, and then fled. Later, the County Public Security Bureau arrested the murderer and sent him to the Baoshan County Government. After several court hearings by Judge Huang Jie, the case was concluded and sentenced the day before yesterday. The murderer Qian Jisheng was sentenced to death for the crime of premeditated murder and deprived of his civil rights indefinitely. Zhou Wang was acquitted. After the verdict in this case, Qian Jisheng refused to accept the sentence and filed an appeal yesterday. The reason he gave was that he was indeed instigated by his lover Zhou Wang, and that's why he did it. It was not his intention at first. He met with the woman twice in Huatian and Yangmu Bridge to negotiate. The woman was an accomplice and should have been found guilty. Therefore, he was dissatisfied. After the judge Huang received the appeal from the suspect, he had already prepared the case files and sent them to the High Court for review.

Live-in Son-in-law Requests to Live Separately from His Wife's Family 148

Liu Guangcai, the live-in son-in-law of Wang Zhonglin, said that he has been living in his wife's family for a long time and has to be subject to their control. He discussed with his wife, Wang Caiyuan, about moving elsewhere. When Wang Zhonglin and his wife heard about this, they thought that this move by their son-in-law was inconsistent with their original intention of recruiting him as a live-in son-in-law, so they tried their best to stop him. Liu then filed a lawsuit with the Special Zone Local Court, claiming that his parents-in-law were obstructing his freedom and requesting permission to move elsewhere with his wife. During the hearing the other day, Wang Caiyuan testified that her husband wanted to leave her parents because he had other affairs. However, she really did not want to abandon her parents and go out with her husband. Her husband had taken away many of her clothes and accessories, and she requested that he be ordered to return them. Liu Guangcai insisted that his wife should live with him elsewhere. Judge Zhou ordered them to retire and wait for a scheduled sentence.

Xia Shaoen is the Assassin of Zhao Zheng 151

Proven by Zhao Tieqiao's Wife▲Formerly a Patrol Team Soldier of the China Merchants Bureau

▲Dismissed Last October Due to an Incident▲The Reason for Assassinating Zhao was that He was Instigated by Someone

Xia Shaoen, the assassin of Zhao Tieqiao, the commissioner of the China Merchants Bureau, has been interrogated repeatedly by the County Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Jinghua after being brought back from Hefei, Anhui. His confession has been very detailed. There are now clues regarding the beginning and end of the assassination of Zhao, and it has been found that Xia Shaoen was a policeman in the Sixth District Public Security Bureau in the 17th year of the Republic of China and was changed to a soldier in the China Merchants Bureau's patrol team in the 18th year of the Republic of China. He was dismissed in October last year, but the name of Xia Shaoen still exists on the current roster of the China Merchants Bureau's patrol team. According to Xia's confession, the reason for assassinating Zhao this time was that he was instigated by someone. Director Shen took a photo of the assassin Xia to the Zhao residence on Rue Lupan yesterday. Zhao Tieqiao's wife personally identified whether he was the assassin, as Mrs. Zhao was an eyewitness at the scene of the incident. According to the results of the identification, it was indeed the assassin, and she saw him fleeing after firing the gun. Therefore, the beginning and end of the Zhao case and the content of its background should be revealed to the world in the next few days.

Robbers Demand Money in Cold Weather 152

▲Open Fire if Not Given ▲Husband and Wife, Hu Yiyuan, Injured

Hu Yiyuan (also known as Datongyuan), a native of Ningbo, 54 years old, residing at No. 69, Jin Yang Lane, Pei Kai Er Road, Tilanqiao, has been a money exchanger at the pier and has some savings, which made him the target of bandits. Around 12:30 yesterday afternoon, two thugs, speaking the Shanghai dialect, wearing dark gray wool and cotton clothes, broke into his house and asked if Datongyuan was home. At that time, Hu was upstairs and answered. The robbers said, "The weather is getting cold, please lend us some money." After Yiyuan refused, the robbers took out a gun to threaten him. His wife, Zhou (47 years old), seeing this, shouted "robbers!" The robber then opened fire on her. Hu quickly covered her with his hand, and the bullet pierced his left arm. A stray bullet also wounded Zhou's lower body. Since it was noon, neighbors heard the gunshot and gathered. Fearing that detectives would come, the robbers fired another shot to show their power and fled. Nothing was lost in the house. Someone called the police at Station 1711, and they rushed to the scene and sent the two injured people to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

▲Three American Women Arrived Suddenly During a Drinking Session▲Blood Stains All Over His Back After the Fight

Around 4 AM yesterday, an Englishman named Kincaid from the Hongkou Huishan Police Station came to the Si Hai Cafe on Broadway with a friend. After a while, three American women suddenly arrived. The Detective of the Water Police Team Acted Lawlessly 154

▲The Municipal Government Advised the Provincial Government to Move the Water Police Team Out of Shanghai

The Second Squad of the Third Team of the First District of the Jiangsu Water Police Team was originally stationed in the Beixinjing area of Shanghai. At the beginning of last month, He Zongyu (nicknamed "San Mazi"), who claimed to be a detective of the team, suddenly brought several people with him and handcuffed Chang Baoxian, who worked as a meal provider in the Xihua Yarn Factory, at 10 PM on the 3rd of that month. He accused him of being a communist suspect and demanded money. Chang's wife rushed to negotiate and paid 50 yuan to a Mr. Yuan, who gave it to a Mr. Feng, who then transferred it to Detective Dai of the team, before Chang was released. On the same day, Tang, Officer No. 6 of the team, sent five plainclothes detectives to the Tanjiadu Elementary School on Route Ghisi, Sixth District of Shanghai, and kidnapped teacher Cai Yiqun. Later, he entrusted someone to send a note with the address on it, asking for 300 yuan to redeem him. After the Sixth District of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau found out, they immediately met with Xie Yaozu, the captain of the Third Team of the Jiangsu Water Police, and went to the headquarters of the Second Squad of the Water Police. They indeed found a person named Cai Yiqun and asked the captain of the squad, Zhu Yanling, for the reason for the detention. According to reports, Chang and Cai were reported by Dai Guangru, a detective of the squad, based on information from informants, and were suspected of being communists, so he specially led the team. Captain Xie said that the squad leader had not reported beforehand, and the team headquarters was not aware of the matter, which was absurd. He immediately sent the squad leader Zhu Yanling to the team headquarters for inspection and took the detective Dai into custody, ordering him to hand over the informants for investigation. He also took Chang and Cai, and He Zongyu, who was accused of helping to arrest people, to the Sixth District and handed them over to the Public Security Bureau for preliminary interrogation. According to Chang and Cai, they were both arrested by the Jiangsu Water Police and extorted heavily. According to He Zongyu, he was instructed by Dai Guangru, a detective of the Second Squad of the Third Team of the First District of the Jiangsu Water Police, to arrest Chang and Cai and detain them upstairs in the squad for extortion. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau believed that Detective Dai Guangru had overstepped his authority and abused his power, which was unforgivable. The squad leader Zhu Yanling did not stop the detective from detaining residents for extortion, which was like kidnapping, and he was also guilty of harming the people and could not escape responsibility. The bureau immediately sent He Zongyu to the Shanghai Local Court for legal interrogation. It also reported to the municipal government to transfer to the Jiangsu Provincial Government that the Jiangsu Water Police Team had repeatedly arrested people in Shanghai without authorization, disturbed local residents, infringed on rights, and exceeded limits. Now that the squad leader Zhu Yanling, detective Dai Guangru, and others dared to openly kidnap people, the local public security was responsible and could not remain silent. The details were reported to the municipal government to transfer to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering the team headquarters to be moved out of the Shanghai area and strictly ordering the direct superiors of the team to severely punish them to warn against illegal activities and maintain officialdom.

Zhou Yongkui Embezzled Consolation Money in the Car Accident Death Case 157

▲Du, a philanthropist, is worthy of admiration ▲Zhou Yongkui is truly insane and mad

At about 2 PM on the 1st of this month, a woman of about thirty years old was hit by a car near Songshan Road in the French Concession and sent to Renji Hospital, where she soon died. Her body was sent to the Tongren Fuyuantang morgue for examination. At that time, the deceased was found to be wearing a dark blue padded jacket and pants. Because there were no relatives, the mortuary coffined her, took photos, and kept her in the hall for claiming. The details were reported in the newspapers on the 2nd. Until the 3rd, after seeing the report, the family members, an old woman and a man, went to Fuyuantang to inquire. According to the old woman, her name was Chen Jin, 60 years old, from Fenghua, and currently lived at No. 223, Yuanfu Lane, Tangshan Road, Hongkou. On the morning of the 1st, her daughter-in-law, Chen Kangyuexiang, went out to collect money and never returned. She saw in the newspaper that a woman was hit by a car on Songshan Road and died, so she came to identify her. She pointed to the man who came with her, saying that he was her son, Chen Xiangzhong (34 years old), who was working as a waiter on a Citibank ship. The staff of Fuyuantang showed her the photos, and she identified that it was indeed her daughter-in-law. She immediately went to the police station. It was found that the driver of the car that caused the accident was named Yang Awu, and the car was owned by a Liu family. So, they requested justice. The driver Yang Awu said he knew a younger brother who was now working as a driver for Commander Liu Zhilu. Yang asked him to ask Commander Liu to ask Mr. Du Yuesheng to mediate. At that time, the family members consulted with relatives and friends. A friend of the same village, Mr. Jia, who worked as a tea room in the Asia Hotel on Sanma Road, heard about it and stepped forward, saying that Zhou Yongkui, a shareholder of the Asia Hotel, was very social and had a close relationship with Mr. Du. If he could be appointed to mediate, it would be resolved satisfactorily. They immediately consulted with Zhou, who readily agreed. The next day, he went to Du's residence on Avenue Haig, after submitting his card, Mr. Du, not knowing the person, asked his friend Yuan Shanbao and lawyer Jin Yu to meet him. After talking, he learned that he had come for the Chen family's matter. Mr. Du agreed to give 400 yuan as consolation money. The family members expressed their gratitude and agreed. Mr. Du entrusted this matter to lawyer Jin. The next day, Zhou Yongkui accompanied the family members to the French Concession to request cancellation of the case, then went to lawyer Jin's office to receive the consolation money. Lawyer Jin paid 400 yuan in full, and Zhou wrote a receipt as proof. Unexpectedly, after ten days, the family members did not receive a penny. They repeatedly asked Zhou, who made all kinds of excuses and even used intimidation. Fortunately, Chen had a cousin, Chen Chuanfu, who was a red gang tailor at the headquarters of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps and was familiar with Mr. Qiu Zijia, a Shanghai gentleman. Knowing that Mr. Qiu was closest to Mr. Du, he asked Mr. Qiu to inquire about the situation. Mr. Du was surprised and asked Mr. Jin and Yuan. Lawyer Jin immediately showed Zhou's handwritten receipt. All three made it clear that they knew that Zhou intended to embezzle the consolation money. So, the night before, he invited Zhou to the Brahma Palace Garden Hotel and questioned him face to face. Zhou still fabricated excuses, saying that he had received the money but it was suddenly stolen on the way. Mr. Jin and Yuan were furious, saying that Zhou's attempt to embezzle the consolation money was insane and mad, and his behavior was worse than kidnapping and robbery. They called the police and arrested Zhou and took him to the police station. Lawyer Jin filed a complaint with the French Public Concession according to Article 356, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, requesting severe punishment.

The Result of the Lawsuit Involving Dalun Goods Hitting Reefs and Insurance Companies 158

▲Yu Ning Loses After Appeal▲Should Be Liable for Compensation

Last year, Dalun Company on Fuzhou Road, Xizhonghe Lane, delivered 30 pieces of cloth to the Pingfu steamboat to be transported to Sichuan. The goods were insured against water damage with the Asuxiulunsi Yu Ning Insurance Company on Hankou Road. Later, the Pingfu steamboat ran aground upstream of Yichang. The captain and others went ashore, and the goods on the ship were looted by local hooligans, who set fire to the boat. Afterwards, Dalun claimed the insured money from Yu Ning Company. The company believed that the incident was the same as piracy. The articles in the insurance policy clearly stipulated that piracy was not covered by insurance and refused to compensate. Dalun hired lawyer Shen Yuesheng to sue in the former Provisional Court, and the defendant lost the case. The defendant refused to accept and filed an appeal. The High Court Branch has completed the trial and concluded that the defendant's appeal was unreasonable and rejected it, and the judgment was sent to both parties. There are many concise words in the judgment, such as "This court ruled that pure piracy is not covered by the insurance scope stipulated in the insurance policy, but the looting in this case was entirely due to the steamboat running aground. In other words, if it were not for the running aground, there would be no looting. The running aground is the cause, and the looting is the result, so there is a causal relationship. The appellant should be liable for compensation for the damage."

Lawsuit to Return Children and Dowry After Divorce 159

Shi Mengying, a native of Changzhou, previously married Li Chundi from the same village. However, Shi had another concubine. After living together for several years, on July 1st of this year, Li and her lover Wu Linbing had a secret meeting in Room 7 of the Industry and Commerce Hotel in the French Concession, forgetting about home. Shi also filed a lawsuit in the Special District Local Court, requesting permission to divorce, which has been judged to be allowed. All of Li's dowry was ordered to be returned. On the 11th of this month, Li's sentence was completed. After her release, she hired lawyer Lu Qi to file a lawsuit in court, requesting that Li's son Yin Cai, daughter Su Ying, and utensils and clothes be returned to the plaintiff. One of the two children is being raised by him, and the other is being raised by his brother's concubine in the countryside. The plaintiff is a child bride and has no dowry. After mutual arguments between the lawyers of the two parties, the court ordered the debate to be concluded and set a date for pronouncement.

Widow Accuses Father-in-Law of Unequal Property Distribution 160

The Cai Hongda dowry shop on Dongjie Street in Xiaodongmen, this city, is an old shop of more than 20 years. It was founded by Cai Lanzhou from Pudong, and its business is very prosperous, with very thick accumulation, and it is the leader in the dowry industry. Now Cai's eldest daughter-in-law, Cai Zhao, and her son Cai Qiyan Qian Baojing, have filed a lawsuit in the local court against her father-in-law Cai Lanzhou for unequal property distribution, concealment, and bias, requesting equal distribution according to shares. Her statement roughly stated that the plaintiff's mother and son, that is, the defendant's eldest daughter-in-law and eldest grandson, the defendant had three sons, the eldest being Jingxian, who died on the fourth day of the fifth month of last year, who was the plaintiff Zhao's husband and Guoqi's father, the second being Langxian, and the third being Chengxian. In July of the year before last, when Jingxian was still alive, due to separate living and cooking, the defendant allocated goods from the Hongda branch, about 6,000 yuan, as independent operating capital. Unfortunately, Jingxian died of illness in less than a year, causing huge losses. Hongda Jingji closed down as a result, leaving debts of about 20,000 yuan, which could not be cleared. At that time, the defendant was afraid of being implicated and proposed analysis as a preparation to resist the creditors' pursuit. Although there was a proposal to establish a basis for allocation, the assessed value of the property was too different, and many omissions were made, which was too biased, and the distribution was uneven, so the agreement was not approved and the signature was refused. The defendant had promised that once Hongda Jingji's affairs were clear, the distribution could be discussed again. Unexpectedly, creditors soon filed lawsuits one after another, and there were as many as nine civil and criminal cases, which completely sealed and sold all the property of the plaintiff's shop, and the compensation was settled. As a result, the plaintiff had no place to live, no food to eat, and life was difficult to describe. Therefore, a request was made for formal analysis according to the previous agreement. Unexpectedly, the defendant reneged on his previous words, using the previous analysis as a basis to resist and ignore it. It was found that the total amount of the defendant's own property, in addition to the capital surplus of Huatai Renji, which was about 12,000 yuan, allocated to his daughter, and the rest of the Hongda, Hongyuan, inventory, property, houses, bases, hui money, and shares, which were known to people, amounted to about 135,000 yuan, and 3,000 yuan was set aside for Chengxian's tuition. According to the original agreement, four shares were allocated, and each share should be 26,700 yuan, but the plaintiff, in addition to the previous receipt of 6,000 yuan for the inventory of Hongda Xinhao and the defendant's payment of 2,700 yuan for the case, still needed to claim 18,000 yuan, but was ignored, causing the plaintiff's mother and son to be separated and dependent on others, living with relatives, with no food or clothing, in difficult circumstances and life was difficult. The defendant, as the senior elder, and the proposer of the initiative to analyze, the plaintiff was the eldest daughter-in-law and eldest grandson, although one was a step-wife and the other was an orphan grandson, they were both juniors. How could they bully the widows and orphans alone, and embezzle the property that should be obtained, concealing and biasing, which was unfair to both reason and law, etc. The defendant Cai Lanzhou also hired lawyer Huang Han and submitted a defense, roughly stating that the plaintiff Cai Zhao had previously colluded with the creditors, hid shop goods, and fabricated 3,000 yuan in false accounts, and made unscrupulous demands on relatives, and that the shop's business was not well managed, leading to this failure, etc. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Keqian specially opened the seventh court to hear the case. The plaintiff Cai Zhao recounted the previous situation, followed by the defendant Cai Lanzhou, 68 years old, a local, with three sons, the eldest having passed away, and the third son, Chengxian, currently twelve years old, born to his second wife, while the eldest and second sons were born to his first wife. In 17 years of the Republic of China, when the eldest son Jingxian was still alive, he had already been divided, with three rooms allocated, each room receiving 8,000 yuan, but the third room received an additional 3,000 yuan as tuition fees in addition to the 8,000 yuan. (Question) How much property do you have? (Answer) Less than 30,000 yuan. I am now helping the youngest room, so I eat and use in the youngest room. (Question) Was there a basis for the allocation? (Answer) It was not established at the time, but it was established in September of the 18th year, when the eldest son had passed away. The judge obtained the statement and tried to mediate, but both parties refused, so they ordered both parties to invite relatives to mediate. If the mediation failed, they would reconvene on a scheduled basis and decide according to law.

Yu Susun Received a Threatening Letter 161

▲Related Person Zhang Chungui Arrested▲But There Are Still Suspicious Points

A few days ago, the owner of Jiangdong Bookstore in Zhangchuan Alley, Yu Susun, reported to the Second District, First Precinct, that yesterday afternoon, he received a threatening letter sent by the post office, demanding to borrow 1,000 yuan in foreign currency, and arranged to meet at the pavilion on the sixth floor of the Little World from 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM on the 15th of this month, using umbrellas and perfume bottles as signals, etc. Because he was unable to comply, he reported for help and attached the threatening letter. After Officer Qian learned of the situation, he immediately notified Yu Susun to return to the store and continue business as usual, waiting for someone to be dispatched to accompany him to the meeting in order to arrest the suspect. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday (the 15th), Officer Qian sent Inspector Qiang Yude, along with plainclothes officers and detectives, to coordinate with the Second Precinct of the First District to assist in the arrest. At that time, they were all disguised in plain clothes and went to the rooftop of the Little World, and sent detectives to hold umbrellas and perfume bottles, waiting specifically. Detectives were scattered everywhere. At 9:50 PM, someone walked onto the roof, as if strolling, and said to the disguised police (i.e., the one holding the umbrella and bottle), "If there is a strong wind, what are you doing here?" As the police were answering, Detective Tang Gengquan went upstairs and apprehended the person. After questioning, he claimed to be Zhang Chungui, currently residing at No. 7, Liangyi Fang. He said that he had returned to Shanghai from Hankou specifically to travel and have fun. Twenty-nine yuan in paper money and four jiao in Hubei provincial notes, a gold-cased watch, and a gold chain were found on his person. He was immediately escorted to his residence in Liangyi Fang for a search. There was only his elderly mother and younger sister at home, but his mother was out. Eighty yuan in paper money and a gold ring (engraved with his name) were found in a box. According to his sister, her brother had indeed returned to Shanghai from Hankou. At the same time, Chen Changfa came to knock on the door, asking what he was doing there so late. He said he came to visit his friend Zhang Chungui. When asked if he knew where Zhang Chungui came from, he said Hankou, but his words were evasive, and he was also taken to the precinct. Officer Qian questioned Zhang Chungui, who claimed that he had returned to Shanghai from Hankou because he had lost money in business in Hankou and came to Shanghai to find other opportunities. He said that the silver dollars in the box were given to him by his other sister, Huayuanyuan, who runs a brothel on Yunnan Road in the British Concession. He insisted that he was indeed sightseeing in the Little World and asked for a thorough investigation. Officer Wang Yufan was dispatched to Huayuanyuan's place for questioning, and it was confirmed that the statement was true, but the amount of money given did not match. However, according to Zhang Chungui, he was indeed sightseeing. Officer Qian felt that although it seemed ordinary, the timing was questionable and could not be rashly judged. It is reported that Zhang Chungui and Chen Changfa, along with the watch, have been sent to the Public Security Bureau for further investigation. It is also rumored that Zhang Chungui and Yu Susun are related by marriage.

Chop Off Index Finger Over Gambling Debt 162

▲Claims it's to Warn Himself in the Future▲Actually Intending to Extort

A local named Wang Gengsheng went to the Renhe Stockade in the Yangxing Street outside the Xiaodongmen in the French Concession last month to gamble, losing 50 yuan. When Wang tried to get the money back but failed, he cut off his own left index finger with a knife, repeatedly threatening. The stockade owner, Zhang Jinsheng, reported the incident, and Wang was arrested and taken to the police station. He was sent to the French Court for investigation the day before yesterday. The plaintiff, Zhang Jinsheng, recounted the previous events. When questioned, Wang Gengsheng admitted that he cut off his finger because he was desperate after losing money and wanted to warn himself against gambling in the future, denying any intention of extortion. Judge Zhu sentenced Wang to seven days of detention. Considering that his finger had already been cut off, the sentence was leniently suspended for two years.

Child Laborer Crushed to Death by Machine 165

Wu Jusheng, a female worker from Nanxun at the China First Hosiery Factory at No. 10 Longjiang Road, Yangshupu, was only fifteen years old. At around 10:00 AM yesterday morning, she was working when, due to a moment of carelessness, her head was caught in the machine. Half of her face was crushed, and her skull burst, a gruesome sight. She died on the spot. The factory's clerk reported the incident to the police station at No. 1287. A car was hired to transport the body to the coroner's office for examination.

Laborer Killed by Car 166

Zhang Guibin, a 46-year-old laborer from Jiangbei, was walking past No. 76 Avenue Edward VII at around 1:00 PM yesterday when a car with license plate No. 2762 approached from the front. Unable to avoid it in time, he was knocked to the ground, sustaining head injuries. Officer No. 502 from the Great Bell Police Station arrived at the scene, recorded the car's license plate number, and sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of his injuries, he died at 6:45 PM that evening.

Pawnshop Employee Steals Expensive Jewelry and Flees 167

▲Arrested by Detectives in Hospital Yesterday

Cheng Xianzhang, a 28-year-old from Xiuning, Anhui, was a clerk at the Yutai Pawnshop on Fangbang Road in the South City. It is said that the pawnshop was established by a wealthy Anhui merchant, and Cheng is a relative of the pawnshop owner, having worked there for almost five years. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 12th of this month, Cheng suddenly stole gold and pearl jewelry worth six or seven thousand yuan and fled. The pawnshop sent out detectives everywhere and reported the incident to the police station, requesting assistance in the arrest. Yesterday, Li Dingyuan, a detective from the Second Precinct of the First District of the Public Security Bureau, learned that Cheng had initially hidden in the Central Hotel on Six Horse Road after stealing the stolen goods, staying there for several days, and then moved to Room 13 of the Nanyang Hospital in the South City. Detective Li quietly went to the hospital and arrested Cheng, along with police officers Cheng Rufu and Ma Jinyuan. He was taken to the Second Precinct of the First District. After a detailed interrogation by Chief Ma, he was immediately prepared to submit the case to the court for review due to the large-scale theft.

Autopsy of Murder Case in Changan Lane 168

▲Deceased was Prostitute Li Shuangfeng

The female tenant of a kiosk room at No. 2 Changan Lane, next to the Weiyang Grand Theater on Annakin Road in the French Concession, was killed by her lover the day before yesterday. The murderer locked the door and fled. It was not until after 12:00 PM that the landlady's maid, Wu Wangshi, discovered the body and informed the landlady, Xie Zidan, who reported the incident to the French police. Detectives were dispatched to investigate. A prostitute's tax certificate with the name Li Shuangfeng, aged 28, was found in the deceased's short jacket pocket. The detectives took the certificate back to the police station and transported the body to the Tongren Fuyuan morgue for an autopsy. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that Detective Bao found that the deceased was indeed named Li Shuangfeng, 28 years old, from Liyang. She used to be a prostitute at the brothel run by Chen Yuanshi (the current landlady's daughter-in-law) at No. 69 Aige Road. Recently, she and her lover, Wang A'er, rented a kiosk room in the remaining house of the Yuan family, her old employer. Yesterday, the Criminal Section of the French Police reported the case to Judge Zhu, who arrived at the scene at 2:00 PM for an autopsy. Detective Bao explained the previous events. Chen Yuanshi also stated that she was willing to pay for the coffin and funeral arrangements. Judge Zhu ruled that the deceased, Li Shuangfeng, had indeed been stabbed to death with a knife and approved Chen Yuanshi's request to provide a coffin for the burial. The police station was instructed to investigate and photograph the body for the record. When the police were photographing the body, a sailor's knife with a deer bone handle, about two inches long and with a sharp, bloodstained blade, fell from behind the deceased's head and neck. It is believed to be the murder weapon and was taken back to the police station for safekeeping. Chen Yuanshi then prepared clothing and a coffin for the burial and temporarily placed it in the Yangzhou Guild Hall.

Detective Team Arrests Notorious Robbers 169

Dong Mingde, the leader of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau Detective Team in the South City, received a tip-off the day before yesterday that a group of robbers, including Fu Xiaoyu, were holding a secret meeting at No. 444 Hongfu Lane, Yongxing Road, Zhabei, plotting illegal activities. He immediately led detectives Hu Haishan, Ren Shouzhi, Yu Maolong, Lü Anpu, and Xu Yulin to the house. They apprehended six people on the spot: robbers Fu Xiaoyu, Sheng Yujun, Wang Agui, Wang Sunshun, Yuan Hezhu, and a female robber, Wang Xias. They were all taken back for questioning. Fu claimed to be 35 years old, from Ningbo, and residing at No. 4 Jiuru Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei. He confessed that at around 5:00 AM the day before yesterday, he and Chen Gongbao, Wang Agui, and Wang Sunshun carried pistols to the home of Wang Tongsheng at No. 23 Dachang Lane, Nanmatou, and robbed them of cash and jewelry worth approximately 800 yuan. He had sent 201 yuan of the stolen money and dozens of bullets to his second landlord, Wang, but Wang had absconded with the money upon hearing of the robbery. On another occasion, he and Wang Sunshun robbed the Xinhongyu Wine Shop at No. 13 Nanmatou of over 200 yuan and clothing. About a month ago, he and his friends Lin Geng robbed the home of Du Xian at No. 3 Runde Lane, across from the Nanshi District Court, of about 300 yuan worth of property and jewelry. Later, he and others robbed a certain family on Yuezhou Road, Yuezhou Lane, Beishi, of over 300 yuan. All of the money had been divided and spent. Wang Agui, 38 years old, from Fenghua, stated that he lived at No. 444 Hongfu Lane, Yongxing Road, Zhabei. Wang Sunshun, 44 years old, from Fenghua, and Yuan Hezhu, 32 years old, also from Fenghua and a tailor by trade, all confessed to the details provided by Fu. Sheng Yujun, 35 years old, from Ningbo, who lived at No. 8 Huachang Lane, Qiujiang Road, stated that he had only recently met Wang Agui. On the 13th of this month, he was playing mahjong with his neighbors at home when Wang Agui suddenly brought two pistols and secretly hid them in the stairwell of his house. He was initially unaware of this, but after being informed by his wife, he was shocked. He went to Wang's house that day to urge him to take them away, but was arrested instead. Wang Xia, 45 years old, from Fenghua, said that she was Wang Agui's wife and that she was the one who pawned or exchanged the jewelry and clothing obtained from their illegal activities. The police then went to Sheng Yujun's home and recovered two pistols, and to the Qinghua Silver Shop on Haining Road, where they recovered two gold bracelets and three gold rings that were part of the stolen goods. They also retrieved stolen clothing from various pawnshops. The case was submitted to the Third Section of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for investigation yesterday.

Fire on Medhurst Road 170

At around 7:00 PM last night, a fire suddenly broke out in the overhanging building at No. 508 Medhurst Road, New Gate Road. The fire spread quickly and reached the roof, threatening to engulf nearby buildings No. 509 and No. 510. The New Gate Fire Brigade rushed to the scene and worked hard to extinguish the fire. It was eventually put out after some time. A total of three houses were destroyed.

Arrest of Robbers on North Baoshan Road 171

Recently, a dyeing factory near the railway bridge on North Baoshan Road, Zhabei, purchased twelve new properties. All of the properties near the factory were rented to tenants. Yesterday morning at around 7:00 AM, the local police station, along with all armed members of the Zhabei Security Corps, quietly surrounded the houses. Four robbers and a female robber were arrested in the side rooms. As they were being taken to the Public Security Bureau, another robber entered the house and was also captured. Several Browning pistols and bullets were found. All five male robbers and the female robber were taken to the district office by car for investigation.

Robbers Visit During Memorial Birthday Celebration 172

▲Robbers Opened Fire, Fortunately No One Was Injured

The Tan family at No. 24 Tangjiaqiao House in Pengpu Township were celebrating a memorial birthday the day before yesterday and had hired monks to chant scriptures. At around 7:45 PM, while relatives and friends were having dinner, three robbers suddenly broke in through the back door. Two of the robbers were armed with pistols and fired two shots into the air, warning everyone to remain silent. They robbed the guests of their gold rings, hairpins, jewelry, silver dollars, etc., worth a total of 180 or 190 yuan. As the robbers were leaving, they fired several more shots before fleeing. Officer Lin from the Pengpu Sub-Station of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau, upon receiving the report, led police officers to the scene, but the robbers had already fled. A report was filed with the General Office to investigate and apprehend the robbers.

Special Dispatch

The Invention of Guangshi Textile Machine by a Compatriot 174

Mr. Xing Guangshi from Haimen County, Jiangsu Province, invented a rough draft of the spinning machine, which has been seen in this newspaper a few days ago. Now, let's introduce the details of his ten years of hard work and management as follows:

Mr. Xing Guangshi lamented that our country's yarn industry was still young and that profits were flowing overseas. He also saw the current situation in Shanxi and Shaanxi provinces, where cotton was cheap and yarn was expensive. Therefore, he was determined to invent the most convenient spinning machine to make it easy to promote and sell throughout the country, benefit the people's livelihood, and enrich the country's economy. He then temporarily suspended the research on the invention of the Earth's gravity machine and devoted himself to the work of the spinning machine. Previously, our country already had the manufacture of this yarn machine, but all of them failed because the yarn was uneven in thickness, often broke, and the part for winding and storing cotton strips could not be solved. Mr. Xing then came up with his own ideas, only to deduce the principle of artificial yarn spinning in our country, and engaged in creation and manufacturing. He manufactured the part for winding and storing cotton strips separately. After painstakingly researching and transforming it dozens of times for seven years, he made a wooden eighty-spindle yarn strip machine and a carding machine each. However, it was still not perfect, and the family property was exhausted, and there was no ability to continue. It was suspended for one year. At that time, Huang Changding happened to meet Mr. Xing at the home of Aunt Yang, who was also Mr. Xing's maternal uncle's family, and then they met. After talking, they made a friendship. They learned that he had invented the yarn machine, and it was suspended due to economic difficulties. Huang couldn't help but regret it. At that time, Mr. Huang had something to do in Bianluo, so he resigned from his job and cooperated with him to plan the progress of the machine. Mr. Xing was responsible for manufacturing, Huang was responsible for economy, and planned everything. In the summer of the Republic of China in the seventeenth year, the Haimen area was not peaceful, and the residence was located in a remote rural area, and the transportation was blocked, which was extremely inconvenient. So he moved to Chongming near Shanghai to continue the research, and submitted an application to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for registration. The Ministry ordered the Shanghai Office to send Shou Senxiang, Chen Jingsheng, and Niu Wenyuan to Chongming to test the actual spinning, which was quite satisfactory. However, the carding machine was still in Haimen, and the whole picture was not seen. The Ministry ordered the entire machine to be remade of iron because the machine was made of wood before further processing. Mr. Xing had worked hard for seven years and achieved such results, which was not easy. How could he have the extra strength to remake it? Only because the official orders were there, he could not look forward and backward, so he disregarded the dangers ahead and took risks to proceed, invited workers to engage in remaking, shuttled between the stove fire and the file, either personally or verbally instructed. If there were any difficulties, they would try to solve them to seek improvement. Then he added an insurance mechanism to ensure that the spinning could be continuous. In the summer of the eighteenth year, it was about to be completed, but there were no drawings yet. Yuan Weiqing, a high-achieving student in the Department of Mechanical Engineering of Jiaotong University from the same township, was interested in studying. During the summer vacation, he was invited to Chongming to draw detailed drawings according to the size of the machine. He discussed a lot with Mr. Xing in March, and there were some modifications in between. The hot summer steamed people, and sweat was like rain. Mr. Xing attached great importance to it without rest. In terms of economy, Mr. Huang was responsible for it, but Mr. Xing was also a poor scholar who sold his fields and property to help. Even if he borrowed money from Zhou Shudian, it was still difficult to make ends meet. In order to save money, he recruited rural coppersmiths with low wages to manufacture them. The major casting parts were made by Shanghai Iron Works. Therefore, the parts were extremely crude. Even a small hook often had to be modified and remade four or five times. The parts remade in Shanghai were also out of shape, and had to be filed and padded in many ways to barely assemble them, which made Mr. Xing very anxious, fearing that it would not be able to spin yarn. Just when the yarn strip machine was about to start, the yarn tube lever was shortened by the workers due to negligence. There was no way to lengthen it with his luggage. As a result, he was mentally stimulated, and also witnessed Mr. Huang's embarrassment due to raising funds. He was given extreme unease, resulting in reduced food intake, haggard appearance, sleepless nights, and was about to collapse. The group persuaded him to save energy and rest, and then he was admitted to Shanghai Xusheng Hospital on October 8. After Chen Xusheng's meticulous treatment, his illness was slightly relieved, but his vitality was greatly depleted, his food intake was small, and he was unable to get out of bed. Just when he was celebrating his gradual recovery, he suddenly had cerebral congestion at 4 pm on October 20, which lasted until 9:15 pm. People in the whole city were shocked and mourned for it. At that time, the yarn strip machine had been assembled, but it had not been started yet. Part of the carding machine had not been assembled yet. Huang invited workers to start assembling it. Fortunately, it was successful, and the yarn strips were very uniform, clean, firm, and tough, which was beyond Mr. Xing's expectations during his lifetime. However, due to the crude parts, it was difficult to be very flexible. If all the original drawings could be followed, each part would be flexible, and the results would be even more impressive. The drawings and instructions were submitted to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for registration. The Ministry was examined by the Industrial Products Reward Review Committee. Then, he received the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's Order No. 2135, which said, "For the purpose of following the order, the supplementary payment of Guangshi Spinning Machine drawings should be handled together. It has been sent to the Industrial Products Reward Review Committee for review, and instructions have been given. According to the report of the committee, the structure of the machine is quite ingenious. However, according to the description in the manual, the cutting part is currently equipped with two knives to cut the lint. It should be ordered to modify the lint cutting part of the carding machine and then submit it for inspection." This order was issued because the lint cutting part of the carding machine had not been completed. Because the machine has been successful, but it still needs to be sorted out and improved to be perfect. In the scientific community, it should stand on a special position, and should not be registered hastily for profit. The Engineering Research Institute of the National Central Research Institute was invited to test it. The director Zhou Zijing and Wang Jitong went to test it and praised it greatly, and sent a public letter No. 167, "Sincerely, I have received your letter saying that Xing Guangshi has invented the details of the spinning machine, and please send someone to Chongming to conduct an on-site test to assess it. The director of this institute has accompanied researcher Wang Jitong and textile expert Deng Bangti to conduct a detailed examination of its working condition at the installation site on March 20 and 21, and record the important dimensions, speeds, etc. for discussion. According to the report of the two experts Wang and Deng, if we can continue to study and improve it, it can be applied to areas where cotton is produced but no yarn factories are set up. In addition to copying the original report for delivery, a corresponding letter is hereby replied. Please check it." (See the Monthly Report of the National Central Research Institute, Volume 1, No. 10) Now I heard that Mr. Huang, in order to make the machine perfect, plans to hire experts to sort it out, and contact various parties to raise funds, set up factories to manufacture and promote it, which is really the gospel of our country's industrial sector. Its office is temporarily located at No. 33, Yan Matou, Nanshi, Shanghai.

The Financial Gold Market Fluctuated Violently Last Week 176

▲The gold market was extremely volatile last week. On Monday, the big bank had already lowered its interest rate to 0.0625. Bank of America reduced its interest rate by 0.0125. The standard gold price was still stable in the morning. Then it was heard that Chase Manhattan had dropped as many as 6,000 cash loans. Therefore, people were mentally weak, and large households sold them, plunging more than four taels, and falling to 80 taels. By the afternoon, there seemed to be more buyers, and it was heard that the cash issued by Chase Manhattan was borrowed by Hengxing. The price was on the rise again, totaling more than 85 taels, and closing at 5 taels and 3 qian, which was 2 and a half taels higher than the previous Saturday. There was a difference of 6 taels and 2 qian on that day. The next day, the big bank only reduced the long-term interest rate by 0.0625. It was ordered not to move the previous market, and the later market suddenly changed to reduce the interest rate by half a grade. The internal market was also tight, and the industry was scrambling to settle. As for the gold market, it was firm in the morning and became stronger in the afternoon, reaching 89 taels and 5 qian, because large households were chasing in, and the exchange rate was repeatedly reported lower, especially the peers were psychologically expecting the cash ban to be relaxed. On Wednesday, it suddenly rushed out of the 90 taels mark, and people in the market were firm and bullish, probably because the deadline for the ban on cash exports had arrived, so they imagined that the ban would be lifted, and various firms such as Da Decheng Yuan Mao Yong Zhi Feng Yong and others bought in one after another, with some short covering, so the afternoon reached 92 taels. As a result, it fell sharply by 1 tael, totaling 90 taels and 9 qian, which had risen for three consecutive days, totaling 8 taels and 1 qian. However, the difference on that day was not huge, only about 4 taels, probably because the big bank slightly reduced the interest rate and the foreign exchange market seemed tight. Although the big bank lowered the interest rate the next day, the Japanese-British and Japanese-American markets were lower, so the gold market was initially suppressed, but the foreign exchange market was weak, and speculator Wu sold it. However, Yongheng covered a short position of about 3,000 for Luo, so the price was still able to stand at the 90 taels mark. After the first order and other orders were relaxed, and the sellers were not lazy, they broke the 90 taels mark. The market once looked good in the afternoon, because the bulls deliberately released air, and the swap rate should be raised to 6 or 7 taels, so the shorts did not dare to underestimate it and made some replenishments, and then coaxed it to 91 taels, but the result was again softened to 88 and a half taels, which was 2 taels and 4 qian lower than the previous day, which was the reverse direction of the three-day rise. The silver market rebounded the next day. The first order was extended by half a grade, and the internal market was also tight, so the gold market opened lower. Then it was suddenly heard that Japanese Prime Minister Hamaguchi was assassinated and seriously injured, so people were suddenly mentally weak, and large households sold it, and it plummeted to 81 taels and 2 qian. Later, according to the Osaka telegram, although Hamaguchi's injury was dangerous, there was no danger to his life, so the market situation turned peaceful again, and the swap rate was privately opened by the industry. After the authorities of the exchange persuaded him not to listen, it was raised from 4 or 5 taels to 7 taels, so the market price has been pulled up by more than 6 taels, totaling 87 taels, 5 qian and 6 qian. However, the result was still 1 tael and 2 qian lower than the target day. There were 7 taels and 4 qian changes on that day. Saturday happened to be the official swap rate, which turned from high to low. In the morning, the off-market price was initially 7 taels, and then it fell to 4 or 5 taels, and then from 5 taels to 3 taels. The Dalian gang bulls have all swapped it properly, but it is said that some firms have not swapped it all, and there is no entry or exit in December. Basically, it has been changed to the January period. However, the closing price was 80 taels and 9 qian, which was based on the January listing. Compared with the previous day, it fell by 6 taels and 4 qian, which has been falling for three consecutive days, totaling 10 taels. For half a month in January, there were 5 taels of ups and downs, which had retreated to within 80 taels. The transactions of each firm are still many, it is said.

The Foreign Silver Market Is Consistently Bullish 177

Yesterday's London telegram said that the big bank silver had rebounded. Local Chinese and Indian buyers bought in, and the closing price was flat. The recent rebound was 0.0625, which was 16 pence and 75 cents (equivalent to 1 shilling and 7 pence and 8125 cents in British gold). The long-term rebound was also 0.0625, which was 16 pence and 625 cents. The New York telegram said that the price of American silver also increased by 0.0125, and the spot price was 26 cents and 25 cents. The British currency fell by 0.03125 against the American currency, and the American currency rebounded by 0.03125 against the British currency, both of which were 4 yuan, 8 jiao, 5 fen and 625 cents. The Japanese-American and Japanese-British markets did not move. The London-Shanghai first order was shortened by 0.0625, which was 1 shilling and 7 pence and 5625 cents. The Bombay spot price increased by 1 anna, which was 47 rupees and 14 annas.

The Early and Afternoon Li Dividends Are the Same Price Again 178

Yesterday was Sunday, and the market atmosphere in all aspects was relatively quiet. The foreign li for both the early and afternoon markets was the same, which was 7 qian, 2 fen, 6 li, 1 hao and 2 hu and a half. The silver discount for both the early and afternoon markets was also the same, which was 1 qian and 3 fen. The banks were closed and there was no news to report. The market made remittances and drafts. The early market was 600,500, and the afternoon market was 440,000. The early market for banknotes was 16,000, and the afternoon market was 5,000. The money shops received more than 3.9 million foreign public orders and more than 33 million silver public orders. The remittances from various routes were more than 300,000. The small money shops traded 300,000 to 400,000 subsidiary currency market conditions. The Jiangnan small foreign currency was again 6 qian and 4 fen for both markets. The transaction was 2,000 jiao in the early market and 1,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Silk and Tea: Last Week's Silk Market Increasingly Lifeless 186

▲ Lyons sales stagnant...New York cables show prices declining ▲ Japanese silk price drop unabated...Shanghai mills find it difficult to sell at low prices

Last week, the silk market in Shanghai's foreign firms became increasingly lifeless. Since the financial crisis in Lyons and Marseille, the raw silk market has been virtually without transactions, compounded by severe flooding, which has led to increased mill closures and even weaker silk sales. While New York factories are interested in spring silk futures, the low prices of Japanese silk are fiercely competitive. Cables from China report high prices, resulting in few transactions and declining prices, particularly for Shanghai-produced silks. Economic instability is also evident in Yokohama and other locations, with approximately 60% of silk mills ceasing operations. European sales of Japanese silk have plummeted, and the price decline remains unchecked. Shanghai manufacturers universally report capital depletion. Government bond issuance is still pending. Officials are earnestly encouraging mills to resume operations to maintain employment. Currently, mills are exploring ways to resume production, but their existing silk inventory was acquired at higher costs. The current market is weak, resulting in substantial losses, making sales difficult. Transactions for Sichuan and Anhui silks are also scarce, with only about 100 bales of spot trading throughout the week. Silk exports are limited to 400 bales. Overseas Chinese silk prices have fallen sharply.
